本文件按照 GB/T 1.1 一 202 久标准化工作导则第工部分:标准化文件的结构和起草规则的规定起惠。	This document is drafted in accordance with the provisions of the GB/T 1.1-202 Standardization Work Guidelines Part I: Structure and Drafting Rules of Standardization Documents.	yes
本文件代替 GB 18030 一 2005 信息技术 ”中文编码字符集与 GB 18030 一 2005 相比,除结构调整和编辑性改动外,主要扩术变化如下:	This document replaces GB 18030-2005 "Information Technology - Chinese Encoding Character Set". Compared with GB 18030-2005, besides structural adjustments and editorial changes, the main technical changes are as follows:	yes
增加了本文件适用对象(见第 1 章)，	The scope of this document has been expanded (see Chapter 1),	yes
在双字节编码区更改了 10 个竖排标点和8 个汉字构件所对应的 GB/I 13000 代码位置,并其除了 6 个重复编码的汉字构件和 9 个重复编码的汉字( 见附录 D,2005 年版的附录A)，	In the double-byte encoding area, the GB/I 13000 code positions corresponding to 10 vertical punctuation marks and 8 Chinese character components have been changed, and 6 duplicate encoded Chinese character components and 9 duplicate encoded Chinese characters have been removed (see Appendix D, Appendix A of the 2005 edition),	yes
在四字节编码区更改了18 个 GB/T 13000 代码位置(见附录 D,2005 年版的附录D);	In the four-byte encoding area, 18 GB/T 13000 code positions have been changed (see Appendix D, Appendix D of the 2005 edition).	yes
删除了附录 ”追加的汉字及部首/部件 “ 见 2005 年版的附录 〇 ，	The appendix "Additional Chinese Characters and Radicals/Components" has been removed, see the appendix in the 2005 edition.	yes
增加了实现的级别 " (见第9草);	The implemented level has been added "(see Draft 9);	yes
增加了资料性附录 “通用规范汉字表 ; 议字的代码位置 “ 见附录刁。	The informative appendix "General Standard Chinese Character Table; Code Position of the Proposed Characters" has been added, see Appendix D.	yes

GB 18030 一 2022	GB 18030-2022	yes
信息扩术 ”中文编码字符集	Information Expansion "Chinese Character Encoding Set	yes
1 本文件规定了信息技术用的中文图形字符及甚二进制编码的十六进制表示 。	1 This document specifies the hexadecimal representation of Chinese graphic characters and binary encoding used in information technology.	yes
本文件适用于中文和其他文字图形字符信息的处理、交换、存储、传给、显现 、输入和输出。	This document is applicable to the processing, exchange, storage, transmission, display, input and output of Chinese and other text graphic character information.	no
本文件适用于为具备中文和其他文字图形字符信息化处理及交换功能的技术类产品,包括但不限于以输入法、光学字符识别 (OCR)、编辑 校对、机融翻诺、语音合成、文字转写、乔能写作等为代表的软件产品 , 以及以计算机、通信终端设备、电子书阅读毅、学习机等为代表的便件产品 。	This document is applicable to technical products with Chinese and other text graphic character information processing and exchange capabilities, including but not limited to software products represented by input methods, optical character recognition (OCR), editing and proofreading, machine translation, speech synthesis, text transcription, intelligent writing, etc., and hardware products represented by computers, communication terminal equipment, e-book readers, learning machines, etc.	no
2 规泄性引用文件	2 Normative reference documents	no
下列文件中的内容通过文中的规范性引用而构成本文件必不可少的条款。	The contents of the following documents constitute essential provisions of this document through normative references.	no
其中, 注日期的引用文件,仅该日期对应的版本适用于本文件;不注日期的引用文件,其最新厂本(包括所有的修改单)适用于本文件。	For the referenced documents with dates, only the version corresponding to the date applies to this document; for the referenced documents without dates, their latest version (including all amendments) applies to this document.	no

3 术语和定义	3 Terms and definitions	no
下列本语和定义适用于本文件 。	The following terms and definitions apply to this document.	no
3.1 字符 character	3.1 Character	no
供组织、控制或表示数据用的元素集合中的一个元素。	An element in a set of elements used for organizing, controlling or representing data.	no
3.2 编码字符 coded character	3.2 Coded character	no
字符 (3.1) 及其编码 示。	Character (3.1) and its encoding.	no
3.3 用户自定区 private use area	3.3 Private use area	no
使用符合本文件的产品的使用者可以自行规定的区域。	An area that users of products compliant with this document can define themselves.	no
3.4 字汇 repertoire	3.4 Repertoire	no
用编码字符 (3.2) 集表示的一个指定的字符(3.1)集合 。	A specified set of characters (3.1) represented by a set of coded characters (3.2).	no
3.5 保 区 reserved zone	3.5 Reserved zone	no
留作未来本文件规定的区 域 。	An area reserved for future provisions of this document.	no
GB 18030 一 2022	GB 18030-2022	no
4 字汇	4 Vocabulary	no
4.1 概述	4.1 Overview	no
本文件收录的字符以单字节、双字或四字节编码 。	The characters included in this document are encoded in single-byte, double-byte or four-byte.	no
单字节部分收录了 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的 0x00~0x7F 全部 128 个字符 。	The single-byte part includes all 128 characters from 0x00 to 0x7F in GB/T 11383-1989.	no
4.3 双字节部分	4.3 Double-byte part	no
双字节部分收录了 GB/T 2312 一 1980 中的全部图形字符 GB/T 13000 中的CJK 统一汉字以及部分图形字符。	The double-byte part includes all graphic characters in GB/T 2312-1980, CJK Unified Ideographs in GB/T 13000 and some graphic characters.	no
双字节部分的字符按照附录 A 的规定。	The characters in the double-byte part are according to Appendix A.	no
其中,表意文字描述符的图形、代码位置和功能应符合附录 B 的规定 。	The graphics, code positions and functions of ideographic description characters should comply with Appendix B.	no
注: GB/T 13000 对中国、日本、恩国、越南等国家和地区使用的汉字统一编码。	Note: GB/T 13000 unifies the encoding of Chinese characters used in China, Japan, South Korea, Vietnam and other countries and regions.	no
具备独有抽象字形的汉字,赋予单独的代码位置;来源不同而抽象字形相同的汉字, 则赋予共用的代码位置。	Chinese characters with unique abstract glyphs are assigned separate code positions; Chinese characters with the same abstract glyphs from different sources are assigned shared code positions.	no
经过编码的汉字称为CJK 统一汉字 CCJK Unified Ideographs,其中 CJK 表示中国、日本、韩国。	Encoded Chinese characters are called CJK Unified Ideographs, where CJK stands for China, Japan, and Korea.	no
4.4 四字节部分	4.4 Four-byte part	no
四字节部分收录了上述双字节字符之外的 GB/T 13000 中的 66 个CJK统一汉字(9FA6 一 9FEF，不包括 9FB4~9FBB 的8个字符)、CJK 统一汉字扩充 A、CJK 统一汉字扩充 BCJK 统一汉字扩充 C、 CJK 统一汉字扩充 DCJK 统一汉字扩充下 .CJK 统一汉字扩充 F 和已经 在 GB/ 工 13000 中编码的少数民族文字的字符。	The four-byte part includes 66 CJK Unified Ideographs in GB/T 13000 that are not included in the above-mentioned double-byte characters (9FA6-9FEF, excluding 8 characters from 9FB4 to 9FBB), CJK Unified Ideographs Extension A, CJK Unified Ideographs Extension B, CJK Unified Ideographs Extension C, CJK Unified Ideographs Extension D, CJK Unified Ideographs Extension E, CJK Unified Ideographs Extension F and characters of minority languages that have been encoded in GB/Work 13000.	no
四字节部分的字符按照附录 C 的规定 。	The characters in the four-byte part are according to Appendix C.	no
5 总体结构	5 Overall structure	no
正文中凡数字前标有 0x 的表示采用十六进制,未标有 0x 的表示采用十进制。	In the main text, numbers prefixed with 0x are in hexadecimal, and those without 0x are in decimal.	no
附录中凡编码的表示均采用十六进制,其他数字的表示均采用十进制。	In the appendix, all encodings are in hexadecimal, and all other numbers are in decimal.	no
单字节部分采用 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的编码结构,使 用 0x00~0x7F 码位。	The single-byte part uses the encoding structure of GB/T 11383-1989, using the code positions 0x00~0x7F.	no
双字贡部分采用两个八位二进制位串表示一个字符,其首字节码位从 0x81 一 0xFE, 尾字节码位分别是 0x40 一 0x7E 和 0x80 一 0xFE。	The double-byte part uses two eight-bit binary bit strings to represent a character, with the first byte code positions from 0x81 to 0xFE, and the second byte code positions are 0x40 to 0x7E and 0x80 to 0xFE.	no
四字节部分采用 GB/工 11383 一 1989 未采用的 0x30 一 0x39 作为对双字节编码扩充的后缀,编码范围为 0x81308130 一 0xFE39FE39。	The four-byte part uses the unused 0x30 to 0x39 in GB/Work 11383-1989 as the suffix for expanding the double-byte encoding, with the encoding range from 0x81308130 to 0xFE39FE39.	no
四字节字符的第一个字厄编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第二个字记编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39; 第三个字节编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第 四个字市编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39。 即 : 0x81308130 一 0x81308139; 0x81308230 一 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 一 0x8130FE39 ; 0x81318130 一 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c “0URo23061393 0xFE39FE30 一 0xFE39FE39 。	The encoding range of the first byte of the four-byte character is 0x81 to 0xFE; the second byte is 0x30 to 0x39; the third byte is 0x81 to 0xFE; the fourth byte is 0x30 to 0x39. That is: 0x81308130 to 0x81308139; 0x81308230 to 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 to 0x8130FE39; 0x81318130 to 0x81318139; 0x81318230 to 0x81318239 0xFE39FE30 to 0xFE39FE39.	no
总体结构与码位范围分配见图 1 和表 1。	The overall structure and code position allocation are shown in Figure 1 and Table 1.	no
6 字符的排列顺序	6 Character arrangement order	no
6.1 单字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.1 Single-byte part character arrangement order	no
单字记部分字符按照 GB/I 11383 一 1989 中相应字符的顺序排列 。	The characters in the single-byte part are arranged in the order of the corresponding characters in GB/I 11383-1989.	no
6.2 双字市部分字符的排列顺序	6.2 Double-byte part character arrangement order	no
双字下部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 A。	The character arrangement order of the double-byte part should comply with Appendix A.	no
6.3 四字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.3 Four-byte part character arrangement order	no
自 0x81308130 至 0x8439FE39 共 50400 个码位,对应双字节部分未包括的所有 GB/T 13000 基本多文种平面的字符,按照GB/T13000 基本多文种平面相应字符的顺序排列 。	From 0x81308130 to 0x8439FE39, a total of 50400 code positions, corresponding to all characters in the GB/T 13000 basic multilingual plane not included in the double-byte part, are arranged in the order of the corresponding characters in the GB/T 13000 basic multilingual plane.	no
自 0x90308130 至 0xE339FE39 共 1058400 个码位用于对应 GB/T 13000 的16个辅助平面,字符排列顺序完全按照 GB/I 13000 的 16个辅助平面的相应码位顺序依次排列 。	From 0x90308130 to 0xE339FE39, a total of 1058400 code positions are used to correspond to the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/T 13000, and the character arrangement order is completely arranged in the order of the corresponding code positions of the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/I 13000.	no
四字节部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 C。	The character arrangement order of the four-byte part should comply with Appendix C.	no

8 部分字符和代码的说明	8 Explanation of some characters and codes	yes

9.1 通则	9.1 General rules	yes
本文件规定三个实现级别。	This file specifies three implementation levels.	yes
符合相应实现级别的系统软件产品,应提供相应实现级别范围内全部字符的输入输出功能。	System software products that comply with the corresponding implementation level should provide input and output functions for all characters within the scope of the corresponding implementation level.	yes
9.2 实现级别 1	9.2 Implementation Level 1	yes
实现级别 1 文持本文件的单字节编码部分、双季节编码部分和四字下编玛部分的 CJK 统一汉字 ( 即 0x82358F33 一 0x82359636) 和 CJK 统一汉字扩A( 即 0x8139EE39 一 0x82358738) 。	Implementation Level 1 supports the single-byte encoding part, double-season encoding part, and four-character encoding part of this file's CJK unified Chinese characters (i.e., 0x82358F33 - 0x82359636) and CJK unified Chinese characters extension A (i.e., 0x8139EE39 - 0x82358738).	yes
任何本文件适用的产品均应满足实现级别 1 的要求。	Any product applicable to this file should meet the requirements of Implementation Level 1.	yes
注: 根据软件应用需要 ,实现级别 1 还可选择文持表 3 列出的任何一种或多种非汉字文种。	Note: According to software application needs, Implementation Level 1 can also choose to support any one or more non-Chinese languages listed in Table 3.	no
9.3 实现级别 2	9.3 Implementation Level 2	no
实现级别 2 包含实现级别 1。	Implementation Level 2 includes Implementation Level 1.	no
此外 ,实现级别 2 还文持《通用 规范 汉字 表 }中的没有包合在实级别 1 之内的编码汉字。	In addition, Implementation Level 2 also supports the encoded Chinese characters in the "General Specification Chinese Character Table" that are not included in Implementation Level 1.	no
《 通用规范汉字表) 所收汉字在本文件中的代码位置和字形, 见附录下。	The code positions and forms of the Chinese characters collected in the "General Specification Chinese Character Table" in this file are seen in the appendix.	no
系统软件及支撑软件,应满足实现级别 2 的要求 。	System software and supporting software should meet the requirements of Implementation Level 2.	no
注: 系统软件及文撑软件包括但不限于操作系统,数据库管理系统.中间件( 软件产品分类的信息见 GB/ 工 36475)。	Note: System software and supporting software include but are not limited to operating systems, database management systems, middleware (information on software product classification see GB/Work 36475).	no
9.4 实现级别 3	9.4 Implementation Level 3	no
实现级别 3 包含实现级别 2。	Implementation Level 3 includes Implementation Level 2.	no
此外,实现级别 3 还文持本文件规定的全部汉字及表 3 中的康黑部首。	In addition, Implementation Level 3 also supports all Chinese characters specified in this file and the Kangxi radicals in Table 3.	no
用于政务服务和公共服务的产品应满足实现级卉 3 的要求。	Products for government services and public services should meet the requirements of Implementation Level 3.	no
注: 政务服务和 共服务行业包括但不限于铁路运输业.道路运输业 \ 水上运输业.航空运输业、多式联运和运输代理业、邮政业、货币金融服、保险业、土地、管理业、卫生、国家机构、社会保障等 (行业分类的信息见 GB/ 工 4754)。	Note: Government services and public services industries include but are not limited to railway transportation, road transportation, water transportation, air transportation, multimodal transportation and transportation agency, postal services, monetary finance, insurance, land, management, health, national institutions, social security, etc. (information on industry classification see GB/Work 4754).	no

描述 (DESCRIPTION) C 和 C++ 编译器是集成的.他们都要用四个步骤中的一个或多个处理输入文件: 预处理(preprocessing), Hii(compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking) .	DESCRIPTION: C and C++ compilers are integrated. They both process input files in one or more of four steps: preprocessing, Hii (compilation), (assembly) MERE (linking).	yes
源文件后级名标识源文件的语言, 但是对编译器来说, 后绥名控制着缺省设定:	The suffix of the source file identifies the language of the source file, but for the compiler, the suffix controls the default settings:	yes

在连接阶段中,所有对应于源程序的.e 文件，-1 库文件, 无法识别的文件名(包括指定的.o H 标文件和 .a 库文件)按命令行中的顺序传递给连接器选项 (OPTIONS)	During the linking phase, all .e files corresponding to the source program, -1 library files, unrecognizable file names (including specified .o H tag files and .a library files) are passed to the linker options (OPTIONS) in the order of the command line.	no
选项必须分立给出 : de ' 完全不同于 `-d -r '.	Options must be given separately: de ' is completely different from `-d -r '.	no

如果只操作四个阶段( 预处理, 编译, 汇编, 连接)中的一部分, 可以使用 ` -x' 选项 (或文件名后 Ah) 告诉 geo 从哪里开始,用 `~-c' ，`-s' ,或 `-E' 选项告诉 geo 到哪里结束.注意,某些选项组合 (例如 ，`-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c 编译或汇编源文件, ETER. If you only operate part of the four stages (preprocessing, compiling, assembling, linking), you can use the `-x' option (or file name suffix Ah) to tell geo where to start, and use the `~-c', `-s', or `-E' option to tell geo where to end. Note that some option combinations (such as `-x cpp-output -E') {i gee MEF =c compile or assemble source files, ETER. ERA ATI By default, GCC replaces the source file name suffix with `.o' and `.ec' tag file name. You can use the -o option to choose another name. GCC ignores any unrecognized input after the -ec option -S F What's the matter.	yes

编译后即停止, 不进行汇编件.	Stop after compilation, do not assemble.	yes
在编译过程的不同阶段间使用管道而非临时文件进行工作, 因为那些系统的汇编器不能从管道读取数据，GNU 的汇编器没有这个问题，汇编器能够接受的 C "方言 ": 支持符合 ANSI 标准的 C 程序.	Use pipes instead of temporary files between different stages of the compilation process, because those system assemblers cannot read data from pipes, GNU assemblers do not have this problem, assemblers can accept C "dialect": support ANSI standard C programs.	yes
这样就会关闭 GNU Cc 中某些不兼容 ANSI Cc 的特性关键字, 以及诸如 unix 和 vax 这些表明当迎和极少使用的 ANSI trigraph 特性,以及禁上尽管使 用了(译注 :宿主环境 (hosted environment) 下所有的标准库可用，main 函数返回 一个 int 值, 典型例子是除了内核以外几乎所有的程序.对应的独立环境 (f£reestanding environment) 不存在标准库, 程序入口也不一定是 main, 最明显的例子就是操作系统内核.详情参考 gcc 网站最近的资料)	This will turn off some features in GNU Cc that are not compatible with ANSI Cc, as well as keywords such as unix and vax that indicate rare use of ANSI trigraph features, and despite the use of (note: all standard libraries are available in the hosted environment, the main function returns an int value, typical examples are almost all programs except the kernel. The corresponding freestanding environment does not have standard libraries, the program entry is not necessarily main, the most obvious example is the operating system kernel. For details, refer to the latest information on the gcc website)	yes
对于没有参数的函数声明, 例如 `int foo ();', 按 C 风格处理 --- 即不说明参数个数或类型. (仅针对 C++) .	For function declarations without parameters, such as `int foo ();', handle it in C style --- that is, do not specify the number or type of parameters. (Only for C++).	no
正常情况下, 这样的函数 foo 在 C++ 中意味着参数为空.	Normally, such a function foo in C++ means that the parameters are empty.	no
节清单从这里删到试图支持传统 C 编译器的某些方面.	The section list is deleted from here in an attempt to support some aspects of traditional C compilers.	no
详见NU c 手册,我们已经把细节删除, 这样当内容过时后, 人们也不会 HERI.	See the NU c manual, we have deleted the details, so when the content is outdated, people will not HERI.	no
除了一件事: 对于 c++ 程序 (不是C)，` -traditional' 选项带来一个附加效应,允许对 this 赋值.	Except for one thing: for c++ programs (not C), the `-traditional' option brings an additional effect, allowing assignment to this.	no
他和`-Ethis-is-variable' 选项的果一样.	He and the `-Ethis-is-variable' option have the same effect.	no
-traditional-cpp 试图支持传统 Cc 预处理器的某些方面.	-traditional-cpp tries to support some aspects of traditional Cc preprocessor.	no
特别是上面提到有关预处理器的内容, 但是不包括 `-traditional' 选项的其他效应.	Especially the content mentioned above about the preprocessor, but does not include other effects of the `-traditional' option.	no
-fdollars-in-identifiers 允许在标识符 (identifier) 中使用 `$' 字符 (仅针对 C++) .	-fdollars-in-identifiers allows the use of `$' characters in identifiers (only for C++).	no
你可以指定 `“-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' 选项显明禁止使用 `$' 符.	You can specify the `-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' option to explicitly prohibit the use of `$' symbols.	no
(GNU C++ 在某些目标系统缺省允许 `$' 符, 但不是所有系统.)	(GNU C++ allows `$' symbols by default on some target systems, but not all systems.)	no
-fenum-int-equiv 允许 ant 类型到枚举类型 (enumeration) 的隐式转换 (MEF c++) .	-fenum-int-equiv allows implicit conversion from ant type to enumeration type (only for c++).	no
正常情况下 GNU C++ 允许从 enum 到 int 的转换,反之则不行.	Normally, GNU C++ allows conversion from enum to int, but not the other way around.	no
-fexternal-—templates 为模板声明 (template declaration) 产生较小的代码 (仅限于 c++)，方法是对于每个模板函数 (template function),只在 定义他们的地方生成一个副本.	-fexternal-—templates generates smaller code for template declarations (only for c++), by generating only one copy at the place where they are defined for each template function.	no
想要成功使用这个选项, 你必须在所有使用模板的文件中,标记`#pragma implementatio'(定义)或 `#Pragma interface'(声明).	To successfully use this option, you must mark `#pragma implementation' (definition) or `#Pragma interface' (declaration) in all files using templates.	no
程序用 `-fexternal-templates ' 编译时, 模板实例 (template instantiation) 全部是外部类型.你必须让需要的实例在实现文件中出现.	When the program is compiled with `-fexternal-templates', all template instances are of external type. You must make the required instances appear in the implementation file.	no
可以通过 typedef 实现这一点, 他引用所需的每个实例.	This can be achieved through typedef, which refers to each required instance.	no
相对应的, 如果编译时使用缺省选项 ` -fno-exteznal-templates', 所有模板实例明确的设为内置.	Correspondingly, if the default option `-fno-external-templates' is used during compilation, all template instances are explicitly set to built-in.	no
所有的成员函数(除了构造子函数和 mnew 或 delete 成员操作符) 视为所在类的虚函数.	All member functions (except constructors and mnew or delete member operators) are considered virtual functions of the class they belong to.	no
这不表明每次调用成员函数都将通过内部虚函数表.	This does not mean that every call to a member function will go through the internal virtual function table.	no
有些情况下, 编译器能够判断出可以直接调用某个虚函数; 这时就直接调用.	In some cases, the compiler can determine that a virtual function can be called directly; in this case, it is called directly.	no
-fcond-mismatch 允许条件表达式的第二和第三个参数的类型不匹配.	-fcond-mismatch allows the second and third parameters of the conditional expression to be of different types.	no
这种表达式的值是 Void.-fthis-—is-variable 允许对 this 赋值 (仅对 c++).	The value of such an expression is Void.-fthis-—is-variable allows assignment to this (only for c++).	no
合并用户自定义的自由存储管理机制到 c++ 后,使可赋值的`this' 显得不合时宜.	After merging the user-defined free storage management mechanism into c++, the assignable `this' seems outdated.	no
因此, 默认情况下, 类成员函数内部对 this 赋值是无效操作.	Therefore, by default, assigning to this inside a class member function is an invalid operation.	no
然而为了向后兼容, 你可以通过 `-fthis-is-variable' 选项使这种操作有效.	However, for backward compatibility, you can make this operation valid through the `-fthis-is-variable' option.	no
-funsigned-char 把 char 定义为无符号类型,如同 unsigned char.	-funsigned-char defines char as an unsigned type, like unsigned char.	no
各种机器都有自己缺省的 char 类型. 既可能是 unsigned char 也可能是 signed char.	Various machines have their own default char types. It could be either unsigned char or signed char.	no
理想情况下, 当依赖于数据的符号性时, 一个可移植程序总是应该使用 signed char 或 unsigned chaz.	Ideally, a portable program should always use signed char or unsigned char when depending on the sign of the data.	no
但是许多程序已经写成只用简单的 char, 并且期街这是有符号数(或者无符号数, 具体情况取决于编写程序的目标机器).	But many programs have been written to use just char, and they expect it to be a signed number (or an unsigned number, depending on the target machine for writing the program).	no
这个选项, 和它的反义选项, 使那样的程序工作在对应的默认值上.	This option, and its opposite, make such programs work on the corresponding default values.	no
char 的类型始终应该明确定义为 signed char 或 unsigned char, 即使它表现的和其中之一完全一样.	The type of char should always be explicitly defined as signed char or unsigned char, even if it behaves exactly like one of them.	no
如果没有明确声明 ` signed' 或 "unsigned'修饰符, 这些选项用来定义有符号位域 (bitfield) 或无符号位域.	If no `signed' or "unsigned' modifier is explicitly declared, these options are used to define signed bitfields or unsigned bitfields.	no
缺省情况下,位域是有符号的, 因为他们继承的基本整数类型,如 int,是有符号数，然而, 如果指定了 `-traditional' 选项,位域永远是无符号数.	By default, bitfields are signed, because they inherit from basic integer types, such as int, which are signed. However, if the `-traditional' option is specified, bitfields are always unsigned.	no
-fwritable-strings把字符串常量存储到可写数据段, 而且不做特别对待.	-fwritable-strings stores string constants in the writable data segment, without special treatment.	no
这是为了兼容一些老程序,他们算改字符串常量是一个非常糟糕的想法、`-traditional' 选项也有相同效果.	This is for compatibility with some old programs, they think changing string constants is a very bad idea, the `-traditional' option has the same effect.	no
执行摘要	Executive Summary	yes
新冠肺炎对毒品市场的影响	The Impact of COVID-19 on the Drug Market	yes
其影响可能类似于2008年的经济危机	Its impact may be similar to the 2008 economic crisis	yes
全球性的新冠肺炎疫情已使全世界陷入前所未有的危机。	The global COVID-19 pandemic has plunged the world into an unprecedented crisis.	yes
在许多国家，这一疾病己使医疗服务机构穷于应付，几近崩溃，各国政府实施的限制措施已在全球经济中造成了严重紊乱。	In many countries, this disease has overwhelmed healthcare services, bringing them to the brink of collapse, and the restrictive measures implemented by governments have caused serious disruption in the global economy.	yes
对于毒品市场，这场疫情的影响尚不清楚，也很难预测，但有可能影响深远。	The impact of this pandemic on the drug market is still unclear and difficult to predict, but it could be profound.	yes
一些生产者可能会被迫寻找新的方法来制造毒品，因为限制流动的同时也限制了前体和基本化学品的获取。	Some producers may be forced to find new ways to manufacture drugs, as restrictions on movement also limit the acquisition of precursors and basic chemicals.	yes
贩运者由于旅行限制而无法越境，可能不得不寻找新的路线和方法。	Traffickers, unable to cross borders due to travel restrictions, may have to find new routes and methods.	yes
毒品使用和提供的模式可能会改变，政府的应对能力也可能会受到阻碍。	The patterns of drug use and supply may change, and the government's ability to respond may be hindered.	yes
新冠肺炎带来的转变是前所未有的，但还是可以从以往的危机中吸取一些经验教训。	The changes brought about by COVID-19 are unprecedented, but some lessons can still be learned from past crises.	yes
2008年经济危机后，一些吸毒者开始寻找更便宜的合成物质，使用模式转向注射毒品。	After the 2008 economic crisis, some drug users began to look for cheaper synthetic substances, and the pattern of use shifted towards injecting drugs.	no
与此同时，各国政府削减了与毒品相关的预算。	At the same time, governments around the world cut budgets related to drugs.	no
如果各国政府以同样的方式应对当前的经济衰退，预防吸毒和相关风险行为等干预措施和戒毒治疗服务可能会受到沉重打击。	If governments respond to the current economic recession in the same way, interventions to prevent drug use and related risky behaviors, as well as drug treatment services, may take a heavy hit.	no
此外，拦截行动和国际合作的优先性可能会降低，使贩运者更容易行动。	In addition, the priority of interception operations and international cooperation may decrease, making it easier for traffickers to operate.	no
一些国家有大量毒品通过商业航班走私，预计这些国家的贩毒活动受到的直接影响最大。	Some countries have a large amount of drugs smuggled through commercial flights, and these countries are expected to be most directly affected by drug trafficking activities.	no
有信使将甲基苯丙胺等合成毒品放在随身背包或藏在私人行李中携带，有时数量很大。由于几乎各地都对航空客运实施了限制，利用商业航空旅行供应毒品的活动可能会完全中断。	Couriers carry synthetic drugs such as methamphetamine in carry-on backpacks or hidden in personal luggage, sometimes in large quantities. Due to restrictions on air passenger transport almost everywhere, activities supplying drugs through commercial air travel may be completely interrupted.	no
尽管国际邮政供应链也受到了干扰，但利用暗网和货物邮寄进行贩运的活动可能会增加。	Although the international postal supply chain has also been disrupted, trafficking activities using the dark web and cargo mail may increase.	no
从长远来看，经济衰退和相关的封闭措施可能会打乱毒品市场。	In the long run, economic recession and related lockdown measures may disrupt the drug market.	no
由于不断上升的失业率和缺乏机会，贫困和弱势人群将更有可能以有害的方式吸毒，患上吸毒病症，并转向与毒品有关的非法活动一无论是生产还是运输。	Due to rising unemployment rates and lack of opportunities, the poor and vulnerable are more likely to use drugs in harmful ways, develop drug-related diseases, and turn to illegal activities related to drugs - whether production or transportation.	no
贩毒组织可能会利用这种情况，向脆弱人群提供服务，并招募新成员来壮大队伍。	Drug trafficking organizations may take advantage of this situation, provide services to vulnerable populations, and recruit new members to strengthen their ranks.	no
随着政府应对能力的降低，这些转变可能会快速扎根，成为许多社区的新现实。	As government response capabilities decrease, these changes may quickly take root and become the new reality for many communities.	no
扩张与复杂性	Expansion and Complexity	no
市场增长	Market Growth	no
人口增长模式部分解释了市场扩张的原因	Population growth patterns partly explain market expansion	no
世界各地的吸毒现象一直在增多，无论是从总体数字还是从吸毒者在世界人口中所占比例来看都是如此。	Drug use is increasing worldwide, both in absolute numbers and as a proportion of the world's population.	no
2009年估计吸毒者有2.1亿人，占全球15-64岁人口的4.8%,而2018年估计吸毒者有2.69亿人，占这类人口的5.3%。	In 2009, it was estimated that there were 210 million drug users, accounting for 4.8% of the global population aged 15-64, while in 2018, it was estimated that there were 269 million drug users, accounting for 5.3% of this population.	no
在过去二十年期间，发展中国家吸毒情况的增长速度远远快于发达国家。	Over the past twenty years, the growth rate of drug use in developing countries has far outpaced that in developed countries.	no
这在一定程度上反映了这一期间总体人口增长的差异、发达国家为7%,发展中国家为28%但也反映了发展中国家年 轻人口增长较快。	This to some extent reflects the difference in overall population growth during this period, with developed countries at 7% and developing countries at 28%, but also reflects the faster growth of the young population in developing countries.	no
青少年和年轻成年人在吸毒者中所占比例最大。	Teenagers and young adults make up the largest proportion of drug users.	no
在2000-2018年期间，发展中国家这一年龄段的人口增长了16%,而发达国家这一年龄段的人口减少了10%。	Between 2000 and 2018, the population in this age group in developing countries grew by 16%, while in developed countries it decreased by 10%.	no
1城市化是当前和未来毒品市场的一个驱动因素	Urbanization is a driving factor in the current and future drug market	no
无论是发达国家还是发展中国家，城市地区的吸毒情况都多于农村地区。	Whether in developed or developing countries, drug use is more prevalent in urban areas than in rural areas.	no
吸毒情况总体增多的部分原因是人口从农村向城镇的大规模流动一目前全世界人口有一半以上生活在城市地区，而1960年这一比例为34%。	Part of the reason for the overall increase in drug use is the large-scale movement of people from rural to urban areas - currently more than half of the world's population lives in urban areas, compared to 34% in 1960.	no
城市化可能是毒品市场未来动态的一个关键因素，特别是在城市化趋势更为突出的发展中国家。	Urbanization may be a key factor in the future dynamics of the drug market, especially in developing countries where the trend towards urbanization is more pronounced.	no
财富的增加与吸毒情况增多相联，但承受疾病负担最大的是最贫穷的人在世界范围内，发达国家的吸毒情况比发展中国家更为普遍。	Increased wealth is associated with increased drug use, but the greatest burden of disease is borne by the poorest. Globally, drug use is more common in developed countries than in developing countries.	no
可卡因之类的毒品更是与世界上较富裕的地区联系较为牢固。	Drugs like cocaine are more firmly linked to wealthier regions of the world.	no
同样，在各国内部，社会富裕阶层的吸毒流行率较高。	Similarly, within countries, drug prevalence rates are higher among the affluent social classes.	no
但转为吸毒病症的比率较高的却是社会经济地位较低的人。	However, those with lower socioeconomic status have a higher rate of transition to drug-related diseases.	no
来自少数几个国家的数据表明，有害的吸毒模式与病症同低收入之间存在联系。	Data from a few countries suggest that harmful drug use patterns and diseases are associated with low income.	no
这些模式在较富裕的社会阶层似乎不太常见。	These patterns seem less common in wealthier social classes.	no
全球新冠肺炎危机造成的经济制约很可能会加剧包括吸毒者在内的最弱势群体的风险。	The economic constraints caused by the global COVID-19 crisis are likely to exacerbate the risks for the most vulnerable groups, including drug users.	no
例如，劳动力市场的变化，如失业率上升，过去一直与吸毒情况的增加有关，而这场疫情己经迫使全球数千万人失业。	For example, changes in the labor market, such as rising unemployment rates, have always been associated with an increase in drug use, and this pandemic has already forced tens of millions of people worldwide to lose their jobs.	no
新冠肺炎或将导致毒品市场进一步扩张新冠肺炎的大流行可能会导致更多农民增加或从事非法作物种植，或是因为国家主管机关的控制能力降低，或是因为在经济危机之下可能有更多人不得不铤而走险，从事非法活动。	COVID-19 may lead to further expansion of the drug market. The pandemic may lead to more farmers increasing or engaging in illegal crop cultivation, either because of reduced control by national authorities or because more people may have to take risks and engage in illegal activities in the face of economic crisis.	no
新冠肺炎的相关限制措施导致空中和陆路交通减少，海上贩运可能已经因此而增加，海上的拦截风险低，而且比空中或陆路走私的数量更多。	The COVID-19 related restrictions have led to a reduction in air and land transport, and sea trafficking may have increased as a result, with lower interception risks at sea and larger quantities than air or land smuggling.	no
最近已有报告称可卡因货物直接从南美经由海路运往欧洲。	There have been recent reports of cocaine shipments being sent directly from South America to Europe by sea.	no
复杂性增强	Complexity Enhanced	yes
非国际管制物质的出现情况稳定，但有潜在危害的新型类阿片正在增多毒品市场正日趋复杂。	The occurrence of non-internationally controlled substances is stable, but new types of potentially harmful opiates are increasing, making the drug market increasingly complex.	yes
除大麻、可卡因和海洛因等植物类物质之外，已经增添了数百种合成毒品，其中许多并不在国际管制之下。药品的非医疗使用也快速增多。	In addition to plant substances such as cannabis, cocaine, and heroin, hundreds of synthetic drugs have been added, many of which are not under international control. Non-medical use of drugs is also rapidly increasing.	yes
会员国的国内市场每年约有500种新型活性物质。	Member countries have about 500 new active substances on their domestic markets each year.	yes
目前其中大多是兴奋剂，其次是合成的大麻素受体激动剂和少量的类阿片。	Most of them are currently stimulants, followed by synthetic cannabinoid receptor agonists and a small amount of opiates.	yes
虽然新型精神活性物质的总体数量已经稳定下来，但比例发生了变化。	Although the total number of new psychoactive substances has stabilized, the proportion has changed.	yes
在2014年确定的新型精神活性物质种类总数中，类阿片新型精神活性物质仅占2%,但到2018年，这一数字己上升至9%。	In the total number of new psychoactive substances identified in 2014, new psychoactive opiates accounted for only 2%, but by 2018, this number had risen to 9%.	yes
类阿片新型精神活性物质中有许多是芬太尼的类似物，其药效和危害已得到证明，在北美导致了过量死亡事件，其他区域也有，但程度较轻。	Many of the new psychoactive opiates are fentanyl analogs, whose efficacy and harm have been proven, causing overdose deaths in North America and other regions, but to a lesser extent.	yes
在北美，芬太尼有的用作海洛因和其他毒品（包括可卡因和甲基苯丙胺）的掺杂剂，有的用来制造假冒的药用类阿片。	In North America, some fentanyl is used as an adulterant for heroin and other drugs (including cocaine and methamphetamine), and some is used to manufacture counterfeit medicinal opiates.	yes
一些证据表明，欧洲也有注射新型精神活性物质兴奋剂的现象：一项对欧洲六个城市废弃注射器残留物的研宄发现，许多注射器都沾有产生兴奋作用的新型精神活性物质》	Some evidence suggests that there is also a phenomenon of injecting new psychoactive substance stimulants in Europe: a study of discarded syringe residues in six European cities found that many syringes were contaminated with new psychoactive substances that produce stimulant effects.	yes
2新型精神活性物质的使用可能会逐渐牢固存在于弱势群体中	2 The use of new psychoactive substances may gradually become entrenched in vulnerable groups	no
单一种类的新型精神活性物质几乎从未形成大的市场。	A single type of new psychoactive substance has almost never formed a large market.	no
但来自欧洲的证据表明，合成大麻素在无家可归者和监狱囚犯等社会边缘群体中是一个严重的问题。	But evidence from Europe suggests that synthetic cannabinoids are a serious problem among socially marginalized groups such as the homeless and prison inmates.	no
有22个国家报告了监狱中使用新型精神活性物质的情况，其中大多数国家将合成大麻素确定为主要挑战。	22 countries have reported the use of new psychoactive substances in prisons, with most countries identifying synthetic cannabinoids as the main challenge.	no
对前体化学品的管制迫使制毒者进行创新最常作为前体用来合成苯丙胺、甲基苯丙胺和“摇头丸”等毒品的许多化学品已被置于国际管制之下。	Control of precursor chemicals forces drug manufacturers to innovate. Many chemicals used as precursors to synthesize amphetamines, methamphetamines, and "ecstasy" have been placed under international control.	no
贩毒者和制毒者一直在寻找替代品一不仅有管制较松的物质，还有专门为规避管制而设计的化学品，即所谓的“特制前体”。	Drug traffickers and manufacturers are always looking for alternatives, not only substances with looser controls, but also chemicals specifically designed to evade control, the so-called "specially designed precursors".	no
旨在阻止新冠肺炎传播的限制性措施很可能使依赖前体化学品的制毒者受到进一步挤压。	Restrictive measures aimed at preventing the spread of COVID-19 are likely to further squeeze drug manufacturers who rely on precursor chemicals.	no
来自墨西哥的证据表明，这已经成为 现实：据报告，2020年3月，从东亚进口的甲基苯丙胺前体短缺促使墨西哥和美国的甲基苯丙胺价格上涨。	Evidence from Mexico suggests that this has become a reality: according to reports, in March 2020, a shortage of methamphetamine precursors imported from East Asia prompted a rise in methamphetamine prices in Mexico and the United States.	no
市场瞬息万变	The market is changing rapidly	no
合成药物在中亚和俄罗斯联邦取代阿片剂	Synthetic drugs replace opiates in Central Asia and the Russian Federation	no
中亚和俄罗斯联邦的阿片剂市场在2008年至2018年期间似乎发生了变化。	The opiate market in Central Asia and the Russian Federation seems to have changed from 2008 to 2018.	no
俄罗斯联邦当局截获的阿片剂数量下降了约80%，同时因使用类阿片而接受治疗的人数大幅减少。	The number of opiates intercepted by the Russian Federation authorities has dropped by about 80%, while the number of people receiving treatment for opiate use has significantly decreased.	no
但兴奋剂市场却似乎日渐兴旺。	But the stimulant market seems to be thriving.	no
有证据表明，甲基苯丙胺和各种卡西酮，包括甲氧麻黄酮和 a - 吡咯烷基苯戊酮，现在俄罗斯毒品市场上随处可见。	There is evidence that methamphetamine and various cathinones, including methoxymethcathinone and a-pyrrolidinopentiophenone, are now ubiquitous in the Russian drug market.	no
俄罗斯当局报告称，最近查获的制造各种非法药物的秘密加工点数量急剧上升，在两年内翻了一番多，2018年增至152个加工点。	Russian authorities report that the number of secret processing points for the production of various illegal drugs has surged, more than doubling in two years, increasing to 152 processing points in 2018.	no
阿富汗和伊拉克甲基苯丙胺市场增长	Methamphetamine market growth in Afghanistan and Iraq	no
早在2012年，对医院、监狱和其他机构人员的调查就已经揭示了甲基苯丙胺在伊拉克的重要性。	As early as 2012, surveys of hospital, prison, and other institutional staff had already revealed the importance of methamphetamine in Iraq.	no
结晶甲基苯丙胺已经成为“芬乃他林”和曲马多之外又一种令人担忧的主要药物。	Crystalline methamphetamine has become another major drug of concern, in addition to "phenethylamine" and tramadol.	no
2015年的一项研宄进一步证实了这些发现，吸毒者表示大麻比“芬乃他林”或甲基苯丙胺更难获得。	A 2015 study further confirmed these findings, with drug users stating that cannabis was harder to obtain than "phenethylamine" or methamphetamine.	no
最近，伊拉克当局发现了多个甲基苯丙胺加工点，麻管局已对伪麻黄碱制剂的大批进口表示关切一甲基苯丙胺加工点将这些制剂用作前体。	Recently, Iraqi authorities have discovered multiple methamphetamine processing points, and the Bureau of Narcotics has expressed concern about the large imports of pseudoephedrine preparations - methamphetamine processing points use these preparations as precursors.	no
在阿富汗，甲基苯丙胺制造似乎始于2014年。	In Afghanistan, methamphetamine production seems to have started in 2014.	no
自那时起，甲基苯丙胺的缉获量一直在稳步上升。	Since then, the amount of methamphetamine seized has been steadily increasing.	no
但2019年上半年的缉获量一^657公斤——与上一年相比大幅骤增。	But the amount seized in the first half of 2019 - 657 kilograms - was a sharp increase compared to the previous year.	no
在其他国家大量缉获了据认为源自阿富汗的甲基苯丙胺，这也表明该国的产量正在迅速上升。	Large seizures of methamphetamine believed to originate from Afghanistan in other countries also indicate that the country's production is rapidly increasing.	no
政策变化和变化趋势	Policy Changes and Trends	yes
非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域大多有大麻使用增多的趋势	Most jurisdictions where non-medical use of cannabis is legalized have seen an increase in cannabis use.	yes
加拿大、乌拉圭和美国的11个法域允许制造大麻产品供非医疗使用。	Canada, Uruguay, and 11 jurisdictions in the United States allow the production of cannabis products for non-medical use.	yes
在其中多数法域，大麻使用自合法化以来有所增多，尽管在其他未将非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域也观察到了同样的趋势。	In most of these jurisdictions, cannabis use has increased since legalization, although the same trend has been observed in other jurisdictions where non-medical use of cannabis has not been legalized.	yes
在美国最早通过立法的两个州科罗拉多州和华盛顿州，成年人非医疗使用大麻的情况增加，特别是过去一个月以及每天或几乎每天使用的情况增多，自2012年起便已超过了全国平均水平。	In Colorado and Washington, the first two states in the United States to pass legislation, adult non-medical use of cannabis has increased, especially in the past month and daily or almost daily use, which has exceeded the national average since 2012.	yes
所有指标都显示，自2011年以来，乌拉圭的大麻使用情况有所增加，上月使用情况几乎翻了一番。	All indicators show that since 2011, cannabis use in Uruguay has increased, with last month's use almost doubling.	yes
这表明增加的主要原因是经常和频繁使用大麻。	This suggests that the main reason for the increase is frequent and regular use of cannabis.	yes
加拿大的短期数据也表明，2018年至2019年合法市场扩大的同时，使用量也在增加。	Short-term data from Canada also shows that as the legal market expanded from 2018 to 2019, usage also increased.	yes
然而，2019年仍有40%的大麻使用者靠非法来源获得某些产品。	However, in 2019, 40% of cannabis users still obtained some products from illegal sources.	yes
全球大麻药草缉获量暴跌的背后原因是大麻合法化？	Is the reason behind the global plunge in cannabis seizures the legalization of cannabis?	yes
2018年，全球大麻药草缉获量降至20年来的最低水平，这是因为北美的缉获量下降，在过去10年中下降了 84%。	In 2018, global cannabis seizures fell to their lowest level in 20 years, due to a 84% decrease in North America over the past 10 years.	no
相比之下，同期世界其他地区的缉获量几乎翻了一番。缉获的模式表明，旨在放开大麻市场的政策在下降中发挥了关键作用。	In contrast, seizures in other parts of the world during the same period almost doubled. The pattern of seizures suggests that policies aimed at liberalizing the cannabis market played a key role in the decline.	no
对新型精神活性物质的监管似乎有遏制作用在国内对新型精神活性物质的监管效果仍然很难评估。	The regulation of new psychoactive substances seems to have a deterrent effect, but it is still difficult to assess the effectiveness of domestic regulation of new psychoactive substances.	no
一些对新型精神活性物质采用不同监管制度的国家显示出不同的新型精神活性物质使用流行率。	Countries with different regulatory systems for new psychoactive substances show different prevalence rates of use.	no
在另一些国家，通过国内立法后，新型精神活性物质使用情况有所减少。	In some other countries, the use of new psychoactive substances has decreased after domestic legislation.	no
弱势群体面临合法和非法毒品市场的伤害用于疼痛管理和姑息治疗的药用类阿片主要在高收入国家提供止痛药在各区域分布不均。	Vulnerable groups face harm from both legal and illegal drug markets. Opioids for pain management and palliative care are mainly provided in high-income countries, with uneven distribution across regions.	no
2018年，所有可供医疗消费的药用类阿片中，90%以上在高收入国家。	In 2018, over 90% of all medically available opioids were in high-income countries.	no
大约50%在北美，40%在欧洲，还有2%在大洋洲。	About 50% in North America, 40% in Europe, and 2% in Oceania.	no
这些国家的人口约占全球人口的12%。	The population of these countries accounts for about 12% of the global population.	no
据估计，低收入和中等收入国家的人口占全球人口的88%,但消费的药用类阿片却不到10%。	It is estimated that the population of low- and middle-income countries accounts for 88% of the global population, but consumes less than 10% of medically available opioids.	no
获取药用类阿片的障碍与许多因素有关，包括立法、文化、卫生系统和处方做法。	Barriers to accessing opioids for medical use are related to many factors, including legislation, culture, health systems, and prescribing practices.	no
较贫穷的人患吸毒病症的风险更大2018年约有3,560万人患有吸毒病症。	Poorer people are at greater risk of drug addiction. In 2018, about 35.6 million people had drug addiction.	no
贫困、有限的教育和社会边缘化可能会增加吸毒病症风险，并加剧其后果。高收入国家的研宄证实了这一点，在这些研究中，个人不利的社会经济轨迹一不仅仅是他们在某一时间点的状况一也与吸毒病症风险有关。	Poverty, limited education, and social marginalization may increase the risk of drug addiction and exacerbate its consequences. This has been confirmed by research in high-income countries, where individuals' adverse socioeconomic trajectories - not just their status at a given point in time - are associated with the risk of drug addiction.	no
吸毒病症还会加深社会经济劣势，进一步增加失业、贫困和无家可归的风险，从而助长劣势的恶性循环。这些结果也可能与刑事司法系统内的侮辱性态度和后果有关。	Drug addiction can also exacerbate socioeconomic disadvantages, further increasing the risk of unemployment, poverty, and homelessness, thereby fueling a vicious cycle of disadvantage. These outcomes may also be related to stigmatizing attitudes and consequences within the criminal justice system.	no
妇女、少数民族和移民、性取向多样化群体、因武装冲突或灾难而流离失所的人以及农村环境中的人也可能受到吸毒病症的过重影响，或者在获得治疗服务方面遇到问题。	Women, ethnic minorities and immigrants, diverse sexual orientation groups, people displaced by armed conflict or disaster, and people in rural environments may also be disproportionately affected by drug addiction, or encounter problems in accessing treatment services.	no
根据估计因残疾和过早死亡而损失的健康寿命年数的残疾调整寿命年（DALY)指标，在过去10年中，有害的吸毒对范围更广的社会影响加重。	According to the Disability Adjusted Life Years (DALY) indicator, which estimates the loss of healthy life years due to disability and premature death, the harmful effects of drug use on a wider social impact have increased over the past 10 years.	no
2007年至2018年间，归因于吸毒的全球残疾调整寿命年数增加了 17%。	From 2007 to 2018, the global Disability Adjusted Life Years attributed to drug use increased by 17%.	no
注射吸毒者中常见的未经治疗的丙型肝炎导致的肝癌的相关残疾调整寿命年数增幅特别高——达到40%。	The increase in Disability Adjusted Life Years associated with liver cancer caused by untreated hepatitis C, which is common among injecting drug users, was particularly high - up to 40%.	no
毒品和暴力之间的关系错综复杂很难确定精神活性物质的使用和暴力之间的所有因果关系。	The relationship between drugs and violence is complex and it is difficult to determine all the causal relationships between the use of psychoactive substances and violence.	no
全球范围的有限数据表明，迷醉可能是杀人的一个重要因素。	Limited global data suggests that intoxication may be an important factor in homicide.	no
但在暴力事件中，酒精的作用似乎比毒品更大。	However, in violent incidents, alcohol seems to play a bigger role than drugs.	no
虽然吸毒可能会导致犯罪，但在某些情况下，这种联系可以部分归因于多种中介因素，如社会经济劣势以及由个人风险、家庭环境和同龄人影响造成的其他类型的逆境。	Although drug use can lead to crime, in some cases, this link can be partly attributed to various mediating factors, such as socioeconomic disadvantage and other types of adversity caused by individual risk, family environment, and peer influence.	no
贩毒和暴力之间的联系是多方面的。	The link between drug trafficking and violence is multifaceted.	no
如果已有稳定的犯罪结构，包括国际贩毒在内的大规模有组织犯罪活动有可能在无暴力的情况下实施。	If there is already a stable criminal structure, large-scale organized criminal activities, including international drug trafficking, can potentially be carried out without violence.	no
短期内，暴力的存在和程度与其说取决于贩运的数量，不如说取决于造成有组织犯罪集团之间力量平衡不稳定的某些变化，例如非法市场规模的变化，知名罪犯的死亡或监禁，以及使一个集团弱于另一个集团的执法措施。	In the short term, the presence and degree of violence depend less on the amount of trafficking than on certain changes that destabilize the balance of power among organized crime groups, such as changes in the size of the illegal market, the death or imprisonment of notorious criminals, and law enforcement measures that weaken one group relative to another.	no
最新趋势	Latest Trends	yes
吸毒大麻是最常用的物质，类阿片危害最大	Marijuana is the most commonly used substance, with opioids posing the greatest harm.	yes
据估计，2018年使用大麻的有 1.92 亿人，使之成为全球使用最多的毒品。	It is estimated that in 2018, 192 million people used marijuana, making it the most widely used drug globally.	yes
相比之下，2018年使用类阿片的有5,800万人。	In contrast, 58 million people used opioids in 2018.	yes
但阿片类药物的相关危害却因使用者较少而受到忽视。	However, the associated harms of opioid drugs are often overlooked due to fewer users.	yes
在2017年与吸毒病症有关的估计167,000例死亡中，有66%是这类物质造成的，在据信为吸毒导致的残疾或过早死亡而损失的2,100万年寿命中，有50%是这类物质造成的。	Of the estimated 167,000 drug-related deaths in 2017, 66% were caused by these substances, and of the 21 million years of life lost due to disability or premature death believed to be caused by drug use, 50% were caused by these substances.	yes
合成类阿片的非医疗使用加剧了公共卫生危机	Non-medical use of synthetic opioids has exacerbated the public health crisis.	yes
在西非、中部非洲和北非，加剧类阿片危机的是曲马多；在北美则是芬太尼。这两个区域在经济、人口统计数据或一般吸毒模式方面几乎没有共同点，但都在奋力抗击由容易获得且生产成本低的物质助长的类阿片危机。	In West Africa, Central Africa, and North Africa, the opioid crisis is exacerbated by Tramadol; in North America, it is Fentanyl. These two regions have little in common in terms of economy, demographic data, or general drug use patterns, but both are struggling to combat the opioid crisis fueled by easily accessible and low-cost substances.	yes
在北美，芬太尼等合成类阿片的使用导致了20年来类阿片过量致死人数增加。	In North America, the use of synthetic opioids like fentanyl has led to an increase in opioid overdose deaths over the past 20 years.	yes
2018年，在美国登记的67,367例过量死亡中，有三分之二涉及芬太尼。	In 2018, two-thirds of the 67,367 overdose deaths registered in the United States involved fentanyl.	yes
加拿大也报告了类似的结果，只是数字较低。	Canada has also reported similar results, albeit with lower numbers.	no
芬太尼导致过量死亡的部分原因是非法药物市场上的芬太尼药效不可预测。	Part of the reason for fentanyl-related overdose deaths is the unpredictable potency of fentanyl on the illegal drug market.	no
在西非、中部非洲和北非，非医疗用途曲马多的市场已有大幅增长。	In West Africa, Central Africa, and North Africa, the market for non-medical use of Tramadol has seen significant growth.	no
在该区域，接受治疗的曲马多使用病症患者越来越多。	In this region, there are an increasing number of patients with Tramadol use disorders receiving treatment.	no
2017年，全球截获的曲马多数量显著增加，达到125吨以上的峰值。	In 2017, the global seizure of Tramadol significantly increased, reaching a peak of over 125 tons.	no
但2018年，在印度通过一项监管曲马多的新法律之后，全球缉获量降至32吨。	However, in 2018, after India passed a new law to regulate Tramadol, the global seizure volume dropped to 32 tons.	no
促成这两地危机的是制造简单和生产成本低，此外还有对曲马多和许多芬太尼类似物或其前体缺乏国际监管。	The crises in these two places are driven by simple manufacturing and low production costs, as well as a lack of international regulation for Tramadol and many fentanyl-like substances or their precursors.	no
使这两地危机恶化的是这些物质在药品市场和非法市场上都有供应，因而更加难以发现和防止其滥用。	The crises in these two places are exacerbated by the fact that these substances are supplied in both the legal and illegal markets, making it even more difficult to detect and prevent their misuse.	no
兴奋剂使用不断增多	Stimulant use is on the rise	no
兴奋剂领域以可卡因和甲基苯丙胺为主，这两种物质在其主要市场的使用量都在上升。	The stimulant field is dominated by cocaine and methamphetamine, both of which are seeing increased use in their main markets.	no
2018年使用可卡因的约有1,900万人，因为可卡因在北美和西欧颇为流行。	In 2018, about 19 million people used cocaine, as it is quite popular in North America and Western Europe.	no
同年使用苯丙胺的约有2,700万人，其中甲基苯丙胺是东南亚和北美使用最多的苯丙胺类兴奋剂。	In the same year, about 27 million people used amphetamines, with methamphetamine being the most commonly used amphetamine stimulant in Southeast Asia and North America.	no
根据所掌握的多数指标，20年来这两个区域甲基苯丙胺的使用一直在扩大。	According to most indicators available, the use of methamphetamine in these two regions has been expanding over the past 20 years.	no
在一些市场上，可卡因和甲基苯丙胺可以共存，有时是相互替代，这样一种药物的使用量上升时另一种药物的使用量就下降，有时是同时增加和减少以满足同一市场的需求。	In some markets, cocaine and methamphetamine can coexist, sometimes substituting for each other, so that when the use of one drug increases, the use of the other decreases, and sometimes both increase and decrease to meet the same market demand.	no
新冠肺炎使注射吸毒者的风险增高	COVID-19 increases the risk for injecting drug users	no
据估计，2018年注射吸毒的约有1,130万人，全球艾滋病毒感染约有10%是注射吸毒造成的。	It is estimated that in 2018, about 11.3 million people injected drugs, and about 10% of global HIV infections were caused by injecting drugs.	no
注射吸毒者感染艾滋病毒的超过100万人，患丙型肝炎的有550万人。	Over 1 million injecting drug users are infected with HIV, and 5.5 million have hepatitis C.	no
2017年，因吸毒死亡的约有 58.5万人，其中一半死于丙型肝炎引起的肝病，而注射吸毒者的丙型肝炎大多仍未得到治疗。	In 2017, about 585,000 people died from drug use, half of whom died from liver disease caused by hepatitis C, and most injecting drug users with hepatitis C have not yet been treated.	no
5 新冠肺炎限制措施造成的类阿片短缺可能导致使用者代之以酒精或苯二氮类药物等更容易获得的物质，或者将类阿片与合成药物混合。	The shortage of opioids caused by COVID-19 restrictions may lead users to substitute with more readily available substances such as alcohol or benzodiazepines, or to mix opioids with synthetic drugs.	no
随着一些使用者改用注射或更频繁地注射，可能会出现更多有害的使用方式。	As some users switch to injecting or inject more frequently, more harmful methods of use may emerge.	no

Limited reception capacity and overwhelmed immigration authorities in member states cannot prevent refugees from submitting "countless" asylum applications in EU countries. The EU's refugee reception system is in a near "permanent crisis".	yes

Shortly after the start of 2023, the US has been relentless in its efforts to curb the development of China's semiconductor-related industries.	yes
近年来，美国打击中国“芯”发展的动作从未停歇，一边精准打压对华半导体产供链，一边构建“去中国化”的半导体产业链联盟，图谋在先进半导体产业上彻底“甩开”中国。	In recent years, the US has never ceased its efforts to suppress China's "core" development, precisely suppressing the supply chain of China's semiconductor industry on one hand, and building a "de-Sinicized" semiconductor industry chain alliance on the other, aiming to completely "shake off" China in the advanced semiconductor industry.	yes

《办法》规定，参加人可以通过个人养老金资金账户购买个人养老储蓄、个人养老金理财产品、个人养老金保险产品、个人养老金公募基金产品等个人养老金产品。	The "Measures" stipulate that participants can purchase personal pension savings, personal pension wealth management products, personal pension insurance products, personal pension public fund products and other personal pension products through personal pension fund accounts.	no

截至2022年底，个人养老金参加人数1954万人，缴费人数613万人，总缴费金额142亿元。	By the end of 2022, the number of participants in personal pensions was 19.54 million, the number of payers was 6.13 million, and the total payment amount was 14.2 billion yuan.	no

一是稳健性，风险管理机制更加健全，投资策略和理念更为稳健，并实施非母行第三方独立托管。	The first is stability, with a more robust risk management mechanism, more stable investment strategies and concepts, and the implementation of independent custody by non-parent third parties.	no
二是长期性，试点阶段养老理财产品的期限都在5年及以上，下一步发行的个人养老金理财产品，最短持有期原则上为1年，鼓励持有3年以上。	The second is long-term, the term of the pension wealth management products in the pilot stage is all 5 years and above, the next step is to issue personal pension wealth management products, the shortest holding period is in principle 1 year, encouraging holding for more than 3 years.	no
三是普惠性，产品购买门槛低，起购点一般为1元，有的低至0.01元，产品的托管费、管理费等费率更加优惠。	The third is inclusiveness, the product purchase threshold is low, the starting point is generally 1 yuan, some are as low as 0.01 yuan, and the rates of custody fees, management fees and other fees are more favorable.	no
专业人士指出，投资者要根据产品特点和自己的风险承受能力进行选择。	Professionals pointed out that investors should choose according to the characteristics of the product and their own risk tolerance.	no
个人养老金储蓄具有期限较长、利率较高、安全性高的特点，适合风险承受能力弱的人群；个人养老金保险产品重在保障，比较适合无法承担投资风险，可以接受稳定收益的人群；而个人养老金理财产品和公募基金产品不保本也不保收益，有一定投资风险，但预期收益较高，适合具备一定的金融知识、风险承担能力较高的人群。	Personal pension savings have the characteristics of long term, high interest rate, and high safety, and are suitable for people with weak risk tolerance; personal pension insurance products focus on protection and are more suitable for people who cannot bear investment risk and can accept stable returns; while personal pension wealth management products and public fund products do not guarantee principal or income, have certain investment risks, but the expected returns are higher, suitable for people with certain financial knowledge and higher risk tolerance.	no

南京楼市再现“差价赔付”-中新网	"Price Difference Compensation" Reappears in Nanjing Real Estate Market - China News Network	yes
扬子晚报讯(记者 马祚波)扬子晚报/紫牛新闻记者10日在采访中发现，十余年未见的“保价协议”又重回了南京楼市，位于江北新区的一家楼盘宣称“差价赔付”，在交房前其他房源的优惠大于之前的折扣，开发商愿意为买房人换房并退还差价。	Yangzi Evening News (Reporter Ma Zuobo) Yangzi Evening News/Zi Niu News reporter discovered in an interview on the 10th that the "price guarantee agreement" that has not been seen for more than ten years has returned to the Nanjing real estate market. A real estate project located in the Jiangbei New District claims "price difference compensation". If the discounts of other properties before the delivery are greater than the previous discounts, the developer is willing to change the house for the buyer and refund the difference.	yes
“保价协议”条件可不少	There are not a few conditions for the "price guarantee agreement"	yes
这家位于江北新区的楼盘名为保利扬子萃云台，看房人孙先生告诉记者，他在上周末逛楼盘时发现了一则“声明”。	This real estate project located in Jiangbei New District is called Poly Yangzi Cuiyuntai. Mr. Sun, a house viewer, told reporters that he found a "statement" when he visited the real estate project last weekend.	yes
他发给记者的图片上显示，该楼盘的开发商承诺，凡是在2月1日-2月28日期间购买房源的，自双方签订买卖合同之日起至对应房源交付，若该项目其他房源的优惠折扣大于之前购房所享折扣的(限与该商品房属于同一户型、同一楼栋、同一单元、同一物业类型的其他未售商品房)，开发商可以为购房者换房并退还差价。	The picture he sent to the reporter shows that the developer of the project promises that for those who purchase properties between February 1 and February 28, from the date of signing the purchase and sale contract to the delivery of the corresponding property, if the discount of other properties in the project is greater than the discount enjoyed by the previous purchase (limited to other unsold commercial properties of the same type, same building, same unit, and same property type), the developer can change the house for the buyer and refund the difference.	yes
孙先生表示，置业顾问表示这其实就是一份“保价协议”，目的是让买家放心出手，不用担心开发企业降价促销，“现在就怕买完了它就降价了，去售楼处闹吧没时间，不闹的话也确实窝心”。	Mr. Sun said that the property consultant said that this is actually a "price guarantee agreement", the purpose is to let buyers feel at ease, not to worry about the developer's price reduction promotion, "Now I'm afraid that it will reduce the price after I buy it, I don't have time to make a fuss at the sales office, and it's really upsetting if I don't make a fuss."	yes
还有不少买房人则认为，“保价协议”虽然是在给购房者吃“定心丸”，不过条件却不低。	Many homebuyers believe that although the "price guarantee agreement" is to give homebuyers a "reassurance pill", the conditions are not low.	yes
打算在江北买一套刚需房的郑女士说，保价的房源首先是要同一户型，还得在同一楼栋、同一个单元，买家可以比价的房源寥寥，因此“门槛”还是蛮高的。	Ms. Zheng, who plans to buy a just-needed house in Jiangbei, said that the price-guaranteed properties must first be of the same type, and must be in the same building and the same unit. The properties that buyers can compare are few, so the "threshold" is quite high.	yes
也有购房者认为，由于信息不对称，销售时不排除给出额外的让利，买家“维权”的难度不小。	Some homebuyers believe that due to information asymmetry, it is not ruled out that additional concessions will be given during sales, and it is not easy for buyers to "defend their rights".	yes

The total number of transactions in the project is only 33, accounting for only 13%.	no

报告：2022年回国求职留学生数量再创新高-中新网	Report: The number of returning students seeking jobs in 2022 hits a new high - China News Network	yes
2022年回国求职应届留学生留学国前10 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	2022 returning job-seeking graduates from the top 10 study abroad countries. Source: "2022 China Returnees Employment Survey Report"	yes
中新网北京2月11日电 (门睿)近日发布的《2022中国海归就业调查报告》(下称“报告”)显示，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高，我国企业对海外人才的需求亦呈上扬态势。	China News Network, Beijing, February 11th (Men Rui) The recently released "2022 China Returnees Employment Survey Report" (hereinafter referred to as the "Report") shows that the scale of 2022 graduates studying abroad has increased by 8.6% year-on-year, and the number of returning students seeking jobs has hit a new high. The demand for overseas talents by Chinese companies is also on the rise.	yes
报告指出，自2020年以来，在中国国内求职的海归数量明显增长，回国求职的应届留学生数量增多。	The report points out that since 2020, the number of returnees seeking jobs in China has significantly increased, and the number of returning graduates seeking jobs has increased.	yes
与2021年相比，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高。	Compared with 2021, the scale of 2022 graduates studying abroad increased by 8.6% year-on-year, and the number of returning students seeking jobs hit a new high.	yes
从回国求职留学生的留学国家分布来看，英国占比最高，为41.4%，其次是澳大利亚(20.3%)和美国(9%)，排名与2021年一致。	Looking at the distribution of the countries where returning students seeking jobs studied, the UK has the highest proportion, accounting for 41.4%, followed by Australia (20.3%) and the United States (9%), ranking the same as in 2021.	yes
从同比增速来看，2022年来自马来西亚、日本、新加坡的应届留学生人数同比大幅上升，增速分别为66.1%、50.9%和37.7%。	In terms of year-on-year growth rate, the number of 2022 graduates studying abroad from Malaysia, Japan, and Singapore has increased significantly, with growth rates of 66.1%, 50.9%, and 37.7% respectively.	yes
来自加拿大、德国、美国、澳大利亚的应届留学生人数同比下降。	The number of graduates studying abroad from Canada, Germany, the United States, and Australia has decreased year-on-year.	yes
2023春节后第一周海归人才供需走势 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	Supply and demand trends for returnees in the first week after the 2023 Spring Festival. Source: "2022 China Returnees Employment Survey Report"	yes
调研显示，决定回国的留学生中，58%认为“国内生活更加便利”，40%因“更认同国内的文化环境”决定回国，32%认为“国内就业机会更多”，22%认为国内经济活动会加速复苏，能获得更多就业机会。	The survey shows that among the students who decided to return to China, 58% believe that "life in China is more convenient", 40% decided to return to China because they "identify more with the cultural environment in China", 32% believe that "there are more job opportunities in China", and 22% believe that domestic economic activities will accelerate recovery and provide more job opportunities.	yes
数据显示，当前国内企业对海外人才的需求快速释放，对海归人才的需求呈上升趋势。	The data shows that the current demand for overseas talents by domestic companies is rapidly released, and the demand for returnees is on the rise.	no
2023年春节后首周，海归优先的职位数和在国内求职的海归人数均呈上扬态势，2月3日的海归优先职位数比1月28日增长11%，海归求职人数增长27%。	In the first week after the 2023 Spring Festival, both the number of positions preferred by returnees and the number of returnees seeking jobs in China are on the rise. The number of positions preferred by returnees on February 3rd increased by 11% compared to January 28th, and the number of returnees seeking jobs increased by 27%.	no
从行业看，2022年海归优先岗位中，来自教育/培训行业的职位数占比27.8%，位居第一位，专业服务/咨询、互联网/电子商务行业分别以14.3%、11.1%分列二三。	From the industry perspective, in 2022, the number of positions in the education/training industry accounted for 27.8% of the positions preferred by returnees, ranking first, followed by professional services/consulting, and internet/e-commerce industries with 14.3% and 11.1% respectively.	no
近几年在国内求职的海归人数变化 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	Changes in the number of returnees seeking jobs in China in recent years. Source: "2022 China Returnees Employment Survey Report"	no
从薪酬看，海归优先职位的平均招聘薪酬连续三年走高，2022年达14680元/月(人民币，下同)，比2021年的13719元/月增加961元，增长7%。	In terms of salary, the average recruitment salary for positions preferred by returnees has been rising for three consecutive years, reaching 14,680 yuan/month (RMB, the same below) in 2022, an increase of 961 yuan compared to 13,719 yuan/month in 2021, an increase of 7%.	no
分地域看，2022年海归群体前往新一线城市、二线城市和三线及以下城市发展的意愿均有提升，2022年的投递占比分别为31%、15.7%和14.3%，均高于2021年的投递占比。	In terms of regions, the willingness of the returnee group to go to new first-tier cities, second-tier cities, and third-tier and below cities for development has increased in 2022, with submission proportions of 31%, 15.7%, and 14.3% respectively, all higher than the submission proportions in 2021.	no
对于留学的收获，52.7%的海归表示基本符合预期，相比上年(49.9%)提高了2.8个百分点。	Regarding the gains from studying abroad, 52.7% of returnees said that it basically met expectations, an increase of 2.8 percentage points compared to the previous year (49.9%).	no
有28.2%的海归表示高于或远高于预期，这一比例也高于2021年的25.4%。	28.2% of returnees said that it was above or far above expectations, a proportion that is also higher than the 25.4% in 2021.	no

费用省一半甚至更多？	Save half or even more on costs?	yes
河南省规范整合口腔种植医疗服务价格-中新网	Henan Province standardizes and integrates the price of oral implant medical services - China News Network	yes
央视网消息：种植牙是很多缺牙患者的理想选择，但一直以来，动辄上万元一颗的价格让很多患者望而却步。	CCTV News: Dental implants are the ideal choice for many patients with missing teeth, but the price of tens of thousands per tooth has always deterred many patients.	yes
今年以来，随着种植牙集采的加速落地，各地也将种植牙降价提上日程。	Since this year, with the accelerated implementation of centralized procurement of dental implants, various places have also put the price reduction of dental implants on the agenda.	yes
从2月10日起，河南省单颗常规种植牙医疗服务价格全流程调控目标为4300元，单颗常规种植全流程费用不高于调控目标的97%。	Starting from February 10, the full-process price control target for a single conventional dental implant medical service in Henan Province is 4300 yuan, and the full-process cost of a single conventional implant is not higher than 97% of the price control target.	yes
种植牙齿指的是一种以植入骨组织内的下部结构为基础来支持、固位上部牙修复体的缺牙修复方式。	Dental implants refer to a method of repairing missing teeth based on the lower structure implanted in the bone tissue to support and fix the upper dental prosthesis.	yes
记者从郑州大学第一附属医院了解到，以单颗常规种植为例，从种植到最后修复，价格大概要一万六七千元左右。	Reporters learned from the First Affiliated Hospital of Zhengzhou University that, taking a single conventional implant as an example, the price from implantation to final repair is about 16,000 to 17,000 yuan.	yes
患者 何莹：新政策之后，大夫跟我说，像我这种情况差不多就是8000多元、不到1万元，基本上能省一半。	Patient He Ying: After the new policy, the doctor told me that in my case, it would be about 8,000 yuan, less than 10,000 yuan, basically saving half.	yes
在现行项目基础上，河南省还整合确定了“种植体植入费(单颗)”等15个口腔种植类医疗服务价格项目，并统一制定省管公立医疗机构价格和医保支付类别，取消或调整了牙种植体植入术等20个医疗服务价格项目。	On the basis of the current project, Henan Province has also integrated and determined 15 oral implant medical service price items such as "implant implantation fee (single)", and uniformly formulated the price and medical insurance payment category of provincial public medical institutions, and cancelled or adjusted 20 medical service price items such as dental implant surgery.	yes
郑州市医疗保障局医药价格和招标采购处处长 李云杰：受益的主要是四方，一个是医保，医保的支出少了；医院的占压少了，病人会适当增加；对供应商来说得到了一个市场；对我们患者来说是得利最大的一方，植一颗牙的费用可能要减半甚至更多。	Li Yunjie, Director of the Medical Price and Tendering and Procurement Department of Zhengzhou Medical Security Bureau: The main beneficiaries are four parties, one is medical insurance, which reduces the expenditure of medical insurance; the hospital's occupancy is reduced, and patients will increase appropriately; for suppliers, they have gained a market; for our patients, they are the biggest beneficiaries, the cost of implanting a tooth may be halved or even more.	yes
深圳：打造国内第一、世界领先的极速先锋城市-中新网	Shenzhen: Building the fastest pioneer city in China and leading the world - China News Network	yes
中新网2月11日电 据“深圳工信”微信公众号10日消息，深圳市工业和信息化局近日印发《深圳市极速先锋城市建设行动计划》。	China News Network reported on February 11th, according to the "Shenzhen Industry and Information Technology" WeChat public account on the 10th, the Shenzhen Municipal Bureau of Industry and Information Technology recently issued the "Shenzhen Speed Pioneer City Construction Action Plan".	yes
其中提出，2023年底前，建成高速率、大容量、低时延的超级宽带网络，实现“双千兆、全光网、1毫秒、万物联”网络建设目标，打造国内第一、世界领先的极速先锋城市。	It proposes that by the end of 2023, a super broadband network with high speed, large capacity, and low latency will be built, achieving the goal of "double gigabit, all-optical network, 1 millisecond, Internet of Everything" network construction, and building the fastest pioneer city in China and leading the world.	yes
《计划》提出，加快升级千兆光网。	The "Plan" proposes to accelerate the upgrade of the gigabit optical network.	yes
2023年底前，10G PON端口占比达到100%，全光工业园区(产业园区)数量超过100家。	By the end of 2023, the proportion of 10G PON ports will reach 100%, and the number of all-optical industrial parks (industrial parks) will exceed 100.	yes
《计划》要求，全面提升5G网络能效。	The "Plan" requires a comprehensive improvement in the energy efficiency of 5G networks.	yes
研究制定深圳5G网络服务质量规范标准，开展5G网络测试评估，提升5G网络服务质量。	Research and formulate Shenzhen 5G network service quality standards, carry out 5G network testing and evaluation, and improve the quality of 5G network services.	yes
支持基础电信企业加大对重点区域、场所5G网络的优化力度，全年新增5G基站10000个，全市平均下载速率达到500Mbps、上行速率达到100Mbps，重点区域下载速率达到1000Mbps、上行速率达到200Mbps，网络速率和用户体验感大幅提升。	Support basic telecommunications companies to increase the optimization of 5G networks in key areas and places, add 10,000 5G base stations throughout the year, the city's average download speed reaches 500Mbps, the upload speed reaches 100Mbps, the download speed in key areas reaches 1000Mbps, the upload speed reaches 200Mbps, the network speed and user experience are greatly improved.	yes
打造城市级高品质无线局域网。	Build a city-level high-quality wireless local area network.	yes
制定公共场所无线局域网(WLAN)服务规范，推动全市各区人员密集和信息消费需求集中区域WLAN升级，提供千兆接入能力。	Formulate public place wireless local area network (WLAN) service specifications, promote the upgrade of WLAN in areas of the city where people are concentrated and information consumption demand is concentrated, and provide gigabit access capabilities.	yes
依托“深i网”建设全市公共无线局域网统一认证监管平台，实现“一次认证、无感漫游、智能切换”，支持运营主体将具有公共服务能力的社会自建AP(无线接入点)纳入认证监管平台。	Relying on the "Shen iNet" to build a unified authentication and supervision platform for the city's public wireless local area network, achieve "one-time authentication, seamless roaming, intelligent switching", and support operating entities to include self-built APs (wireless access points) with public service capabilities into the authentication and supervision platform.	no
2023年底前，升级接入AP总量不少于2万个。	By the end of 2023, the total number of upgraded access APs will not be less than 20,000.	no
此外，《计划》还提出，建设高品质全光运力网络、构建多层次算力供给体系、加快关键通信网络设施建设、提升互联网应用服务能力。	In addition, the "Plan" also proposes to build a high-quality all-optical transport network, build a multi-level computing power supply system, accelerate the construction of key communication network facilities, and enhance the ability of Internet application services.	no
《计划》明确，协同构建物联感知体系。	The "Plan" clearly states that it will jointly build an IoT perception system.	no
探索以“开源鸿蒙”操作系统为基础，构建城市感知终端建设管理模式，降低对接成本，加快建设城市级物联感知平台，推动市区物联网平台、各领域专业物联网平台网络与数据互联互通。	Explore the use of the "open source Hongmeng" operating system as the basis, build a city perception terminal construction management model, reduce docking costs, accelerate the construction of a city-level IoT perception platform, and promote the interconnection and data interconnection of the city's IoT platform and professional IoT platforms in various fields.	no
深化物联感知在城市管理、民生服务、公共安全、交通出行等领域应用，拓展城市道路、建筑、公共设施等固定感知与智能网联汽车等移动感知采集渠道。	Deepen the application of IoT perception in city management, people's livelihood services, public safety, transportation and other fields, and expand the collection channels of fixed perception and intelligent networked vehicles for city roads, buildings, public facilities, etc.	no
2023年底前，水电气物联网感知终端数量超过900万，打造20个多功能智能杆应用示范项目。	By the end of 2023, the number of water, electricity, and gas IoT perception terminals will exceed 9 million, and 20 multi-functional intelligent pole application demonstration projects will be built.	no
《计划》还提到，加强卫星与地面通信融合应用、布局低空网络基础设施建设、推进海上5G网络深度覆盖。	The "Plan" also mentions strengthening the integration of satellite and ground communication applications, laying out the construction of low-altitude network infrastructure, and promoting deep coverage of offshore 5G networks.	no
同时，推进海上5G网络深度覆盖、构建产业创新发展生态、支持举办顶级赛事和活动。	At the same time, promote deep coverage of offshore 5G networks, build an industrial innovation development ecology, and support the hosting of top-level events and activities.	no

首批56只融资融券标的股票名单以2023年1月31日为计算基准日确定。	The first batch of 56 margin trading target stocks was determined based on the calculation base date of January 31, 2023.	yes

The benign interaction.	no

（德国之声中文网）拜登政府本周五（2月10日）将6个与疑似参与间谍气球计划的中国实体列入黑名单。	(Voice of Germany Chinese Network) The Biden administration will blacklist six Chinese entities suspected of involvement in a spy balloon program this Friday (February 10).	yes
美国商务部表示，这5家中国公司及1家研究机构帮助中国军队现代化，尤其是航空航天项目，包括飞艇和飞机。	The U.S. Department of Commerce stated that these five Chinese companies and one research institution are aiding the modernization of the Chinese military, especially in aerospace projects, including airships and aircraft.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司很难获得美国的技术出口。	Companies on the blacklist will find it difficult to obtain U.S. technology exports.	yes
名单被称为“实体名单”（entity list），入列的公司除非获得美国商务部的特别出口许可证，否则将无法向美国供应商购买技术或商品。	The list is known as the "Entity List", and companies on it will not be able to purchase technology or goods from U.S. suppliers unless they obtain a special export license from the U.S. Department of Commerce.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司是：北京南江空天科技股份有限公司、中国电子科技集团第四十八研究所、东莞凌空遥感科技有限公司、鹰门航空科技集团有限公司、广州天海翔航空科技有限公司和山西鹰门航空科技集团有限公司。	The blacklisted companies are: Beijing Nanjiang Aerospace Technology Co., Ltd., China Electronics Technology Group's 48th Research Institute, Dongguan Lingkong Remote Sensing Technology Co., Ltd., Yingmen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd., Guangzhou Tianhaixiang Aviation Technology Co., Ltd., and Shanxi Yingmen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd.	yes
在此之前，白宫表示考虑做出更广泛措施，“揭露和处理”中国威胁美国国家安全的更大规模监控活动。	Prior to this, the White House indicated that it was considering taking broader measures to "expose and deal with" larger-scale surveillance activities threatening U.S. national security by China.	yes

从现有残骸证据及中国军方的采购平台资讯，美国政府得出结论，认为该气球的制造厂商“跟中国解放军有直接关系”，而且是中国军方批准的供应商。	Based on the evidence from the existing wreckage and information from the Chinese military's procurement platform, the U.S. government concluded that the manufacturer of the balloon "has a direct relationship with the Chinese People's Liberation Army" and is a supplier approved by the Chinese military.	yes
中国外交部发言人毛宁在周五的新闻发布会上表示，关于一只中国无人民用飞艇因不可抗力误入美国领空的意外事件，中方已经多次说明情况、阐明立场。	Chinese Foreign Ministry spokesperson Mao Ning stated at a press conference on Friday that China has repeatedly explained the situation and clarified its position regarding an accidental incident where a Chinese unmanned civilian airship entered U.S. airspace due to force majeure.	yes

60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquakes in the world in the last 60 years	no
智利大地震（1960年）	Chile earthquake (1960)	no
当地时间1960年5月22日下午3点11分，智利瓦尔迪维亚发生人类史上观测记录到的规模最大的地震，地震矩规模为9.5。	At 3:11 p.m. local time on May 22, 1960, the largest earthquake ever recorded in human history occurred in Valdivia, Chile, with a moment magnitude of 9.5.	no
短短十分钟内，瓦尔迪维亚整座城市变为废墟。	Within just ten minutes, the entire city of Valdivia was reduced to rubble.	no
地震之后引发的巨大海啸袭击到智利海岸线，掀起浪高高度是25米高的巨大海啸。	The massive tsunami triggered by the earthquake hit the Chilean coastline, causing waves up to 25 meters high.	no
海啸波及到遥远的日本、菲律宾。	The tsunami affected distant Japan and the Philippines.	no
如此范围的灾难所造成的罹难人数以及经济损失无法精确得知。	The number of casualties and economic losses caused by such a wide-ranging disaster are unknown.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquakes in the world in the last 60 years	no
阿拉斯加大地震（1964年）	Alaska earthquake (1964)	no
1964年3月27日是一个星期五，也是是耶稣受难日。	March 27, 1964, was a Friday and also Good Friday.	no
这一天美国阿拉斯加发生北美洲历史上最大的地震，矩震级达到9.2。	On this day, the largest earthquake in North American history occurred in Alaska, with a moment magnitude of 9.2.	no
直到2006年，阿拉斯加大地震仍然是有纪录以来世界第三大地震。	Until 2006, the Alaska earthquake was still the third largest earthquake on record.	no
地震发生时，太平洋板块和北美洲板块之间的一个断层在威廉王子湾接近学院峡湾的地方断裂。	When the earthquake occurred, a fault between the Pacific Plate and the North American Plate ruptured near Prince William Sound and College Fjord.	no
在大部分的地区这场地震持续了3分钟到5分钟。	In most areas, the earthquake lasted for 3 to 5 minutes.	no
海床位移引发了巨大的海啸，高度为67米。	The displacement of the seabed triggered a huge tsunami, with a height of 67 meters.	no
由于当天是假日，所以学校和许多企业都关闭了。	Because it was a holiday, schools and many businesses were closed.	no
这场大地震最后导致了139人罹难。	The earthquake eventually resulted in 139 deaths.	no
其中9人直接死于地震，其他130人死于地震引发的海啸。	Nine people died directly from the earthquake, and the other 130 died from the tsunami triggered by the earthquake.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquakes in the world in the last 60 years	no
唐山大地震（1976年）	Tangshan earthquake (1976)	no
1976年7月28日，中国河北省唐山市和丰南县在16小时内发生两次7级以上强烈地震。	On July 28, 1976, two strong earthquakes above magnitude 7 occurred in Tangshan City and Fengnan County, Hebei Province, China, within 16 hours.	no
震源距地面23千米。	The epicenter was 23 kilometers from the surface.	no
唐山市全市交通、通讯、供水、供电中断，顷刻间被夷为平地。	The entire city of Tangshan was leveled in an instant, with transportation, communication, water supply, and electricity cut off.	no
140公里外的首都北京也有强烈震感。	There was a strong tremor in Beijing, 140 kilometers away.	no
据官方统计，包括北京、天津在内的所有受灾地区，地震造成242769人死亡，164851人重伤。	According to official statistics, the earthquake caused 242,769 deaths and 164,851 serious injuries in all affected areas, including Beijing and Tianjin.	no
唐山大地震成为中国有记录至今第二多人死亡的地震，仅次于1556年嘉靖大地震。	The Tangshan earthquake was the second deadliest earthquake on record in China, second only to the Jiajing earthquake in 1556.	no
但是有海外科学家估计，这场地震可能造成至少65万人死亡。	However, some overseas scientists estimate that the earthquake may have caused at least 650,000 deaths.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquakes in the world in the last 60 years	no
印度洋大地震（2004年）	Indian Ocean earthquake (2004)	no
2004年12月26日，印尼苏门答腊岛亚齐省西岸160公里处发生地震，震源深度30公里，矩震级9.1到9.3。	On December 26, 2004, an earthquake occurred 160 kilometers off the west coast of Aceh Province, Sumatra, Indonesia, with a depth of 30 kilometers and a moment magnitude of 9.1 to 9.3.	no
地震引发了浪高高度达15到30米的巨大海啸。	The earthquake triggered a huge tsunami with wave heights of 15 to 30 meters.	no
太平洋沿岸总共14个国家被波及，其中受灾严重最严重的地区包括印尼亚齐省、泰国镐立和普吉岛渡假区、斯里兰卡和印度泰米尔邦。	A total of 14 countries along the Pacific coast were affected, with the most severely affected areas including Aceh Province in Indonesia, Hua Hin and Phuket resort areas in Thailand, Sri Lanka, and Tamil Nadu in India.	no
当时正值圣诞节的旅游旺季，受灾地区聚集了大量的旅客和本地居民，导致许多在沙滩上享受假期的旅客和在海边工作的当地人被海啸卷到海底，使这次地震不少人成为失踪者。	At the time, it was the peak tourist season for Christmas, and the affected areas were crowded with a large number of tourists and local residents, resulting in many tourists enjoying their holidays on the beach and local people working by the sea being swept into the sea by the tsunami, making many people missing from this earthquake.	no
据估计，罹难人数和失踪人数至少有30万人。	It is estimated that the number of deaths and missing persons is at least 300,000.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most destructive earthquakes in the world in the last 60 years	no
汶川大地震（2008年）	Wenchuan earthquake (2008)	no
2008年5月12日，中国四川省汶川地区发生大地震。	On May 12, 2008, a major earthquake occurred in Wenchuan, Sichuan Province, China.	no
根据中国地震局的数据，此次地震的面波震级达8.2级、矩震级达8.3级，破坏地区超过10万平方公里。	According to data from the China Earthquake Administration, the surface wave magnitude of this earthquake reached 8.2, the moment magnitude reached 8.3, and the affected area exceeded 100,000 square kilometers.	no
截至2008年9月25日，地震共计造成69227人遇难，17923人失踪，374643人不同程度受伤，1993.03万人失去住所，受灾总人口达4625.6万人。	As of September 25, 2008, the earthquake had caused 69,227 deaths, 17,923 missing, 374,643 injuries of varying degrees, 19.93 million people lost their homes, and the total affected population reached 46.256 million.	no
是中华人民共和国成立以来破坏力最大的地震，也是唐山大地震后伤亡最惨重的一次。	It was the most destructive earthquake since the founding of the People's Republic of China and the deadliest since the Tangshan earthquake.	no
2009年3月，中国国务院宣布将每年的5月12日定为防灾减灾日，加强对民众的教育和对防灾减灾工作的关注。	In March 2009, the State Council of China declared May 12 as the National Disaster Prevention and Reduction Day each year to strengthen education for the public and attention to disaster prevention and reduction work.	no
之后中国多地政府和中小学在每年这一天举行防震演习。	Subsequently, many local governments and primary and secondary schools in China held earthquake drills on this day every year.	no
中小学也开始重视普及“防震减灾”教育。	Primary and secondary schools also began to pay attention to the popularization of "disaster prevention and reduction" education.	no

海地地震（2010年）	Haiti earthquake (2010)	no
2010年1月12日，加勒比海岛国海地发生里氏7.0级的地震。	On January 12, 2010, a magnitude 7.0 earthquake struck the Caribbean island nation of Haiti.	no
震中位于海地首都太子港以西南方25公里，震源距离地表13千米左右。	The epicenter was located about 25 kilometers southwest of the capital, Port-au-Prince, and the focus was about 13 kilometers below the surface.	no
国际红十字会估计，受到地震影响的人口大约为300万。	The International Red Cross estimates that about 3 million people were affected by the earthquake.	no
海地政府公布的确认死亡人数超过20万。	The Haitian government announced that the confirmed death toll exceeded 200,000.	no
海地国内的一些地区，多达90%的房屋在地震中被摧毁。	In some areas of Haiti, up to 90% of the houses were destroyed in the earthquake.	no
虽然国际社会提供了大量援助和支持，但是这个人口过剩腐败横行的贫困国家从未从这场灾难中恢复过来。	Despite a lot of aid and support from the international community, this overpopulated and corruptly impoverished country has never recovered from this disaster.	no

日本东北大地震（2011年）	Tohoku earthquake in Japan (2011)	no
2011年3月11日日本东北地方外海发生矩震级为9.0的大型逆冲区地震。	On March 11, 2011, a large thrust earthquake with a moment magnitude of 9.0 occurred off the coast of the Tohoku region of Japan.	no
震中位于在宫城县首府仙台市以东的太平洋海域，震源深度测得数据为24千米，并且引发最大爬高40.1米的巨大海啸。	The epicenter was located in the Pacific Ocean east of Sendai, the capital of Miyagi Prefecture, with a focal depth of 24 kilometers, and it triggered a huge tsunami with a maximum run-up height of 40.1 meters.	no
这场地震是日本有观测纪录到以来第一个震级超过9的地震。	This earthquake was the first earthquake in Japan with a magnitude over 9 on record.	no
约有2.2万人在灾害丧生，大约40万座建筑被完全摧毁或倒塌。	About 22,000 people died in the disaster, and about 400,000 buildings were completely destroyed or collapsed.	no
福岛第一核电站受地震海啸影响发生泄漏事故。	The Fukushima Daiichi nuclear power plant was affected by the earthquake and tsunami and a leakage accident occurred.	no
这次事故在国际核事件分级表（INES）中被分类为最严重的7级。	This accident was classified as the most serious level 7 in the International Nuclear Event Scale (INES).	no
福岛核事故导致在全世界都测量到微量辐射性物质，包括碘-131、铯-137（半衰期为30年）在内。	The Fukushima nuclear accident resulted in trace amounts of radioactive substances being measured worldwide, including iodine-131 and cesium-137 (with a half-life of 30 years).	no
大量放射性同位素因此核事故释入太平洋。	A large amount of radioactive isotopes were released into the Pacific Ocean due to this nuclear accident.	no
根据联合国的统计，在土叙两国灾区，目前至少有87万人急需食物。	According to United Nations statistics, in the disaster areas of Turkey and Syria, at least 870,000 people are currently in urgent need of food.	no
仅仅在叙利亚，就有多达530万人因为地震而失去家园。	In Syria alone, as many as 5.3 million people have lost their homes due to the earthquake.	no

目前灾区气温低至零下，很多灾民没有住所。	The current temperature in the disaster area is below zero, and many victims have no place to live.	no
