NEWS GOV-MO: 警情通告：司警局呼吁市民提防假冒电讯公司诈骗短讯	NEWS GOV-MO: Police Notice: The Police Department urges citizens to beware of fraudulent text messages impersonating telecommunications companies.	yes
近日司警局接获多宗电信诈骗案，不法分子假冒本澳电讯公司向事主发送附有网站连结的诈骗短信，以积分到期须尽快换领奖赏为饵，诱骗事主登入虚假网站进行兑换。	Recently, the Police Department has received numerous reports of telecommunications fraud. Unlawful individuals are impersonating local telecommunications companies and sending fraudulent text messages with website links to the victims, using the bait of rewards that need to be redeemed as soon as possible due to expiring points, to lure the victims into logging into the fake website for redemption.	yes
事主按指示输入信用卡资料及验证码，随即收到金融机构通知信用卡出现不明消费记录，怀疑信用卡资料经上述网站被盗取。	The victims followed the instructions to enter their credit card information and verification code, and immediately received a notification from the financial institution about unknown consumption records on their credit card, suspecting that their credit card information was stolen through the aforementioned website.	yes
经查，证实相关电讯公司并无发出上述短讯。	Upon investigation, it was confirmed that the relevant telecommunications company did not send the aforementioned text messages.	yes
司警局呼吁市民，如接获类似手机短讯须提高警惕，切勿登入短讯所载网站连结或提供任何个人资料；若被要求提供信用卡资料、帐户交易密码、交易验证码，更要加倍谨慎，防止信用卡被盗刷。	The Police Department urges citizens to be vigilant if they receive similar text messages, do not log into the website link provided in the text message or provide any personal information; if asked to provide credit card information, account transaction password, transaction verification code, be even more cautious to prevent credit card theft.	yes
防骗提示：	Fraud prevention tips:	yes
1. 多关注网络安全资讯，提高个人防范意识；	1. Pay more attention to cyber security information to enhance personal prevention awareness;	yes
2. 切勿随便登入来历不明的网站并在网站内登记个人及信用卡资料，以防遭人盗用；	2. Do not casually log into unknown websites and register personal and credit card information on the website to prevent theft;	yes
3. 警惕假冒网站及钓鱼网站，时刻留意网站网址是否与官方网站完全相符；	3. Be alert to fake websites and phishing websites, always pay attention to whether the website address is completely consistent with the official website;	yes
4. 为手机、移动装置或电脑安装防毒软件，并定期更新；	4. Install antivirus software on your mobile phone, mobile device or computer, and update it regularly;	yes
5. 怀疑遇到诈骗或其他犯罪时，应立即致电司警局防诈骗查询热线8800 7777或报案热线993求助。	5. If you suspect that you have encountered fraud or other crimes, you should immediately call the Police Department's anti-fraud inquiry hotline 8800 7777 or the crime reporting hotline 993 for help.	no

In addition to work meetings and industry discussions during the two-day (10th and 11th) schedule, representatives from the Hong Kong travel agency industry and media visited various tourist attractions, hotels, and tourism-related facilities in Macau in batches. This is to introduce the latest Macau tourism products to the Hong Kong market, while promoting cultural and tourism linkage between the two places, and jointly expanding the "Hong Kong-Macau Joint Tour" market.	yes

援外医疗是我国援外工作的重要内容。	Medical assistance abroad is an important part of our country's foreign aid work.	yes
1963年，我国向阿尔及利亚派出第一支援外医疗队。	In 1963, our country sent the first medical team to assist Algeria.	yes

（综合11日电）	(Comprehensive news on the 11th)	yes
Google新推出的人工智能聊天机器人Bard出师不利，在宣传短片中“答错问题”，导致Google母公司Alphabet股价周三一度急挫8.9%，跌破100美元大关，市值蒸发1100亿美元（约4765亿令吉），截至周五闭市报94.57美元。	Google's newly launched artificial intelligence chatbot Bard got off to a bad start, "answering the wrong question" in the promotional video, causing Google's parent company Alphabet's stock to plummet by 8.9% on Wednesday, breaking the $100 mark, and the market value evaporated $110 billion (about 476.5 billion ringgit), closing at $94.57 on Friday.	yes
市场担心Alphabet不及竞争对手微软。	The market is worried that Alphabet is not as competitive as Microsoft.	yes
根据《路透社》报道，google较早时在社交媒体发布AI聊天机器人Bard的宣传短片，片中有人询问Bard：“我可以告诉我9岁的孩子关于James Webb太空望远镜 (JWST) 的哪些新发现？	According to a Reuters report, Google earlier posted a promotional video of the AI chatbot Bard on social media, in which someone asked Bard, "What new discoveries about the James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) can I tell my 9-year-old child?	yes
”Bard在回答中提到该望远镜曾拍摄到太阳系外行星的第一张照片。	" Bard mentioned in the answer that the telescope had taken the first photo of an exoplanet.	yes
不过，根据美国国家航空航天局资料，太阳系外行星的第一张照片是由欧洲南方天文台的“甚大望远镜”于2004年所拍。	However, according to data from the National Aeronautics and Space Administration, the first photo of an exoplanet was taken by the "Very Large Telescope" of the European Southern Observatory in 2004.	yes

新加坡旅游业复苏强劲 入境旅客比2021年增长19倍	Singapore's tourism industry recovers strongly, with inbound tourists increasing 19 times compared to 2021	yes
（综合11日电）新加坡旅游局近日公布，预计2023年到访新加坡的国际旅客人次可达1200万至1400万，将带来约180亿至210亿新元的旅游收益；旅客人次和旅游收入将恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约67%至75%的水平；2024年旅游业实现全面复苏的可能性很大。	(Comprehensive news on the 11th) The Singapore Tourism Board recently announced that it is expected that the number of international tourists visiting Singapore in 2023 will reach 12 to 14 million, bringing about 18 to 21 billion Singapore dollars in tourism revenue; the number of tourists and tourism revenue will recover to about 67% to 75% of the level before the COVID-19 outbreak in 2019; there is a high possibility of a full recovery of the tourism industry in 2024.	yes
2022年新加坡旅游市场逐步重新启动和恢复。	In 2022, Singapore's tourism market gradually restarted and recovered.	yes
新加坡旅游局最新发布的统计数据显示，2022年入境旅客从2021年的33.06万人次增长19倍，达到630万人次，超越旅游局早前预估的400万至600万人次，游客已经恢复至疫情前33%的水平。	The latest statistics released by the Singapore Tourism Board show that the number of inbound tourists in 2022 increased 19 times from 330,600 in 2021 to 6.3 million, surpassing the earlier estimate of 4 to 6 million by the Tourism Board, and tourists have recovered to 33% of the level before the pandemic.	yes
2022年1月至9月，新加坡旅游收入共计89.6亿新元，预计2022年全年旅游收入可达138亿至143亿新元，比2021年的18.9亿新元增长6倍至7倍，已经恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约50%至52%的水平。	From January to September 2022, Singapore's tourism revenue totaled 8.96 billion Singapore dollars, and it is expected that the total tourism revenue for 2022 will reach 13.8 to 14.3 billion Singapore dollars, an increase of 6 to 7 times from 1.89 billion Singapore dollars in 2021, and has recovered to about 50% to 52% of the level before the COVID-19 outbreak in 2019.	yes
新加坡政府多措并举，加速旅游业复苏。	The Singapore government has taken multiple measures to accelerate the recovery of the tourism industry.	yes
2022年4月，政府宣布拨款近5亿新元用来刺激旅游业复苏。	In April 2022, the government announced a grant of nearly 500 million Singapore dollars to stimulate the recovery of the tourism industry.	yes
旅游局日前宣布，将计划在未来两年从这笔预算中拨出1.1亿新元，推出更多商业和休闲活动吸引旅客回流。	The Tourism Board recently announced that it plans to allocate 110 million Singapore dollars from this budget over the next two years to launch more business and leisure activities to attract tourists back.	yes
为了使健康养生成为新加坡的旅游亮点之一，新加坡旅游局在2022年11月23日发布了一份意向征集活动，计划在新加坡南部海岸开发一个健康养生景点。	In order to make health and wellness one of the highlights of Singapore's tourism, the Singapore Tourism Board launched a call for proposals on November 23, 2022, planning to develop a health and wellness attraction on the southern coast of Singapore.	yes
新加坡旅游局体育与康养旅游执行署长王凌丽说，近年来，越来越多的游客把身体健康放在各项考虑因素的首位。	Wang Lingli, Executive Director of Sports and Wellness Tourism at the Singapore Tourism Board, said that in recent years, more and more tourists have put physical health at the top of their considerations.	yes
在拥有滨海湾花园、滨海堤坝的滨海南区开发一个健康养生景点，有望为新加坡的旅游业和经济作出贡献，让游客在新加坡消费并逗留更久。	Developing a health and wellness attraction in the Marina South area, which has the Gardens by the Bay and the Marina Barrage, is expected to contribute to Singapore's tourism industry and economy, allowing tourists to spend and stay longer in Singapore.	no
新加坡旅游局局长陈建隆表示，未来几年内，健康养生将成为新加坡旅游产品的重要组成部分。	Chen Jianlong, Director of the Singapore Tourism Board, said that in the next few years, health and wellness will become an important part of Singapore's tourism products.	no
新冠疫情提升了公众对于身体和心理健康的认知和需求。	The COVID-19 pandemic has raised public awareness and demand for physical and mental health.	no
为此，过去两年旅游局一直向本地公众和国际游客推广健康养生项目。	For this reason, the Tourism Board has been promoting health and wellness projects to the local public and international tourists for the past two years.	no
2022年6月，新加坡旅游局举办了首届健康养生节，为公众提供了130多项各类健康活动和体验。	In June 2022, the Singapore Tourism Board held the first Health and Wellness Festival, providing the public with more than 130 various health activities and experiences.	no
新加坡将持续为游客提供新的旅行体验。	Singapore will continue to provide new travel experiences for tourists.	no

新加坡旅游业的复苏加快了航空业复苏。	The recovery of Singapore's tourism industry has accelerated the recovery of the aviation industry.	no
数据显示，截至2022年12月18日，樟宜机场客流量强劲复苏，每天接待的乘客已多达15万人次，每周约100万人次，相当于新冠疫情前的75%左右，航空业员工在岗数量也已经恢复到疫情前约90%的水平。	Data shows that as of December 18, 2022, passenger traffic at Changi Airport has strongly recovered, with as many as 150,000 passengers received daily, about 1 million per week, which is about 75% of the level before the COVID-19 outbreak, and the number of aviation industry employees on duty has also recovered to about 90% of the level before the pandemic.	no
数据显示，2022年1月至10月新加坡已接待旅客2360万人次，相当于新冠疫情前的42%，起降航班17万架次，是疫情前的53%。	Data shows that from January to October 2022, Singapore has received 23.6 million tourists, which is 42% of the level before the COVID-19 outbreak, and 170,000 flights have taken off and landed, which is 53% of the level before the pandemic.	no
旅游业快速复苏，也带动了住宿、交通、餐饮和购物等行业的复苏步伐。	The rapid recovery of the tourism industry has also driven the recovery of industries such as accommodation, transportation, catering, and shopping.	no
新加坡政府和旅游业对中国市场寄予厚望。	The Singapore government and the tourism industry have high hopes for the Chinese market.	no

新冠疫情前，中国每年有约360万人次到新加坡旅行度假。	Before the COVID-19 outbreak, about 3.6 million Chinese people traveled to Singapore for vacations each year.	no

柯淑丹指出，接下来，旅游局将密切关注中国针对出境旅行政策进一步释放的信号，以应对游客需求的变化。	Ke Shudan pointed out that next, the Tourism Board will closely monitor signals from China for further relaxation of outbound travel policies to respond to changes in tourist demand.	no
新加坡旅游局除与携程等中国线上旅行平台、旅行社强化伙伴关系外，将针对中国境外游出现的新趋势，积极做好接待中国游客的准备。	In addition to strengthening partnerships with Chinese online travel platforms and travel agencies such as Ctrip, the Singapore Tourism Board will prepare to receive Chinese tourists in response to new trends in outbound travel from China.	no

重阳问答︱如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	Chongyang Q&A | How to view the US non-farm employment data for January exceeding expectations and future trends - Economic Observer Network - Professional Financial News Website	yes
Q：请问重阳投资，如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势？	Q: May I ask Chongyang Investment, how do you view the US non-farm employment data for January exceeding expectations and future trends?	yes
A：2月3日美国劳工部公布2023年1月非农就业数据，新增非农就业51.7万人，大幅高于市场预期的18.9万人；失业率降至3.4%，为近50年以来的最低位；时薪同比增速4.4%，环比增速0.3%，略有放缓。	A: On February 3, the US Department of Labor announced the non-farm employment data for January 2023, with an increase of 517,000 non-farm jobs, significantly higher than the market expectation of 189,000; the unemployment rate fell to 3.4%, the lowest in nearly 50 years; hourly wages increased by 4.4% year-on-year and 0.3% month-on-month, slightly slowing down.	yes
从总量上来看，本次数据存在很多一次性和技术性因素的扰动，比如罢工返岗的教职工、调查统计口径的修正、季调因子的更新，后续可能将有所修正（参考2022年1月新增非农由50.4万人下修至36.4万人），非农就业或不像数据体现的那样强劲。	In terms of total volume, there are many one-time and technical factors disturbing this data, such as returning teachers from strikes, corrections to survey statistics, updates to seasonal adjustment factors, and subsequent corrections may be made (refer to the revision of non-farm additions in January 2022 from 504,000 to 364,000), non-farm employment may not be as strong as the data shows.	yes
从结构上来看，高科技企业裁员影响仍在，但占比较低；高接触性服务业如休闲酒店、教育保健等新增就业大幅回升，数据显示服务业劳动力缺口仍存。	In terms of structure, the impact of layoffs in high-tech companies is still there, but the proportion is low; high-contact service industries such as leisure hotels, education and health care have seen a significant rebound in new jobs, and the data shows that there is still a labor gap in the service industry.	yes
结合同样大超预期的服务业PMI、岗位空缺和劳动力缺口数据的回升和消费信贷数据的强势，我们判断经过极端天气和节假日后美国服务业迎来了快速修复。	Combining the similarly exceeding expectations of the service industry PMI, job vacancies and labor gap data rebounding, and strong consumer credit data, we judge that the US service industry has undergone rapid repair after extreme weather and holidays.	yes
我们认为，在不经过衰退的情况下美国就业市场的供需紧张难以改善。	We believe that without a recession, it is difficult to improve the supply and demand tension in the US job market.	yes
目前美国劳动力市场尚有500余万的供给缺口，而劳动参与率上行缓慢，尤其是25-54岁劳动参与率已经接近疫情前高点。	Currently, there is still a supply gap of more than 5 million in the US labor market, and the labor participation rate is rising slowly, especially the labor participation rate of 25-54 years old is already close to the pre-pandemic peak.	yes
除此之外，由于美国居民超额储蓄和消费信贷的强势，消费需求的强劲将促使紧缩政策对就业市场的影响进一步滞后。	In addition, due to the strong excess savings and consumer credit of US residents, strong consumer demand will further delay the impact of tightening policies on the job market.	yes
美国就业市场供需持续紧张将是2023年美国经济的底色。	The continued tension in the supply and demand of the US job market will be the underlying tone of the US economy in 2023.	yes
叠加目前临近加息结束，通胀预期不断反复，我们对薪资增速的持续下降并不乐观。	Adding to the current near-end of interest rate hikes, inflation expectations are constantly repeating, we are not optimistic about the continuous decline in wage growth.	no
本次数据公布前，美国股债汇市场对于美联储加息路径的预期过于乐观。	Before the data was released, the US stock, bond and foreign exchange markets were too optimistic about the Federal Reserve's interest rate hike path.	no
随着通胀数据的持续改善，美联储在缩短加息步伐的同时还不断维系着市场通胀预期脆弱的平衡，但市场对于美联储偏向鹰派的表述视而不见，不仅预期提前停止加息，还预期年末两次降息。	With the continuous improvement of inflation data, the Federal Reserve is shortening the pace of interest rate hikes while maintaining the fragile balance of market inflation expectations, but the market ignores the Federal Reserve's hawkish statements, not only expecting to stop raising interest rates in advance, but also expecting two rate cuts at the end of the year.	no
在劳动力市场供需紧张，紧缩政策影响不明的情况下，我们认为美联储年末对于加息的指引是相对合理的，市场极端预期的调整和交易的拥挤或将对市场产生一定伤害。	In the case of tight supply and demand in the labor market and unclear impact of tightening policies, we believe that the Federal Reserve's guidance on interest rate hikes at the end of the year is relatively reasonable, and the adjustment of extreme market expectations and crowded trading may cause some damage to the market.	no
尽管如此，薪资增速的顽固难改当前通胀快速下降的趋势，随着M2数据同比转负以及各个CPI分项领先指标的逐渐转好，自10月份以来美国CPI数据已经转向快速下降阶段，薪资增速的顽固仅会对以后的通胀数据形成托底，当前的市场预期难以证伪，在下一期通胀数据公布后市场或进入新一轮博弈。	Despite this, the stubbornness of wage growth is difficult to change the current trend of rapid decline in inflation. With the year-on-year M2 data turning negative and the gradual improvement of various CPI sub-item leading indicators, the US CPI data has entered a rapid decline stage since October, and the stubbornness of wage growth will only form a bottom for future inflation data. The current market expectations are difficult to falsify, and the market may enter a new round of game after the next inflation data is released.	no
杉杉创始人郑永刚因突发心脏疾病过世 曾带领中国服装第一股转型 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	Zheng Yonggang, founder of Shanshan, passed away due to a sudden heart disease. He once led China's first listed clothing company to transform - Economic Observer Network - Professional Financial News Website	yes
经济观察网 记者 郑淯心 2月11日，认证主体为杉杉控股有限公司（以下简称“杉杉控股 ” ） 的微信公众号发布讣告，杉杉企业创始人、杉杉控股董事局主席郑永刚因突发心脏疾病救治无效，于2023年2月10日去世，享年65岁。	Economic Observer Network reporter Zheng Yu Xin, February 11, the WeChat public account certified by Shanshan Holdings Limited (hereinafter referred to as "Shanshan Holdings") announced that Zheng Yonggang, the founder of Shanshan Enterprises and the chairman of the board of directors of Shanshan Holdings, died of a sudden heart disease on February 10, 2023, at the age of 65.	yes
上世纪80年代，郑永刚担任国营棉纺厂的厂长，随着调任，1989年郑永刚成为杉杉股份的前身宁波云港服装总厂的厂长。	In the 1980s, Zheng Yonggang served as the director of a state-owned cotton spinning factory. With his transfer, in 1989, Zheng Yonggang became the director of Ningbo Yungang Garment Factory, the predecessor of Shanshan Shares.	yes
2022年12月，在第二十届中国企业领袖年会暨第二十二届中国企业未来之星年会上，郑永刚在演讲中称，在上世纪90年代的中国西服市场，杉杉品牌的市占率曾高达37 % 。	In December 2022, at the 20th China Enterprise Leaders Annual Meeting and the 22nd China Future Stars Annual Meeting, Zheng Yonggang said in his speech that in the Chinese suit market in the 1990s, the market share of Shanshan brand once reached 37%.	yes
1996年杉杉股份（600884.SH）上市，成为中国服装业第一家上市公司。	In 1996, Shanshan Shares (600884.SH) was listed, becoming the first listed company in China's clothing industry.	yes
就在服装业务如日中天时，杉杉集团却开始转型，因为郑永刚意识到 ， “ 一旦市场放开，中国品牌自然会形成一个梯队式品牌市场，杉杉西服想一直独领风骚，长期成为国人的国服的可能性不大 ” 。	Just when the clothing business was booming, Shanshan Group began to transform, because Zheng Yonggang realized that "once the market is opened, Chinese brands will naturally form a tiered brand market, and it is not likely that Shanshan suits will always lead the trend and become the national dress of the Chinese people in the long term".	yes
1999年，杉杉开始研究企业转型，郑永刚回忆当年 ， “ 我们来到上海，寻求到底转型做什么，专门找了很多专家学者，连续不断地开一些诸葛亮会、务虚研讨会。	In 1999, Shanshan began to study corporate transformation. Zheng Yonggang recalled that year, "We came to Shanghai to find out what to transform, and specifically sought many experts and scholars, and continuously held some Zhuge Liang meetings and theoretical seminars.	yes
最后，我们设定了两个大的战略方向。	In the end, we set two major strategic directions.	yes
第一个方向是新能源新材料，另外一个是大健康有未来 ” 。	The first direction is new energy and new materials, and the other is that big health has a future".	yes
战略方向确定后，杉杉开始寻找合作，那时候鞍山热能院为鞍钢配套的炭素研究所在做国家863课题，科研经费不够，于是杉杉和鞍山热能院碳素研究所签署合作协议，共同推动国家863课题“中间相炭微球”项目产业化，从事负极材料的研发、生产和销售，在国内实现负极材料的商用推广。	After the strategic direction was determined, Shanshan began to look for cooperation. At that time, Anshan Thermal Energy Institute, which was supporting Ansteel, was conducting a national 863 project. The research funding was not enough, so Shanshan and Anshan Thermal Energy Institute Carbon Research Institute signed a cooperation agreement to jointly promote the industrialization of the national 863 project "Intermediate Phase Carbon Microsphere", engage in the research, production and sales of negative electrode materials, and promote the commercial promotion of negative electrode materials in China.	yes
2001年，杉杉股份实现中间相炭微球的规模化生产，开始国产化替代，取代日本成为国内中间相炭微球主要供应商。	In 2001, Shanshan Shares realized the mass production of intermediate phase carbon microspheres, began to replace imports, and replaced Japan as the main supplier of intermediate phase carbon microspheres in China.	no
这是中国第一家锂离子电池负极材料生产企业，实现了锂离子电池负极材料国产化。	This is China's first lithium-ion battery negative electrode material production enterprise, realizing the localization of lithium-ion battery negative electrode materials.	no
随着锂电池的应用迅速普及，杉杉股份的锂电池业务开始逐步发展，2007年锂电材料业务被写入了杉杉股份的主营业务，服装业务营收占比逐年减少，直至2013年，杉杉股份的锂电材料业务收入全面超过服装业务。	With the rapid popularization of lithium batteries, Shanshan Shares' lithium battery business began to gradually develop. In 2007, the lithium battery material business was written into the main business of Shanshan Shares. The revenue of the clothing business decreased year by year. Until 2013, the revenue of Shanshan Shares' lithium battery material business completely surpassed the clothing business.	no
2021年2月，杉杉股份成功并购LG化学偏光片业务，进军LCD偏光片市场，并成立偏光片企业杉金光电，该领域技术含量比较高，杉杉的主要的竞争对手都是世界500强，如韩国三星、日本的住友化学、日东电工。	In February 2021, Shanshan Shares successfully acquired LG Chem's polarizer business, entered the LCD polarizer market, and established a polarizer company, Shangjin Optoelectronics. The technology content in this field is relatively high, and Shanshan's main competitors are all Fortune 500 companies, such as Samsung in South Korea, Sumitomo Chemical in Japan, and Nitto Denko in Japan.	no
郑永刚曾分享过投后管理的心得 ， “ 中国的民营企业收购国际上的一些高科技企业，成功概率比较低，为什么那些收购会失败？	Zheng Yonggang once shared his experience in post-investment management, "The success rate of Chinese private enterprises acquiring some high-tech enterprises internationally is relatively low. Why do those acquisitions fail?	no
因为大家都会去考虑，我花了那么多钱，我得去派人管对吧，这是通常会做的一个行为 ” ， 然而郑永刚则不同，杉杉收购成功的那一天，郑永刚就到杉金光电当众宣布，杉杉作为杉金的大股东，决定实施一企两制，除了郑永刚担任董事长，杉杉企业的人不派到杉金，采取授权经营的方式，原有的分配制度、企业文化、各项管理等模式不变。	Because everyone will consider, I spent so much money, I have to send someone to manage it, right? This is a behavior that is usually done", but Zheng Yonggang is different. On the day Shanshan successfully acquired, Zheng Yonggang publicly announced at Shangjin Optoelectronics that Shanshan, as the major shareholder of Shangjin, decided to implement a one-enterprise-two-systems policy. Except for Zheng Yonggang serving as the chairman, Shanshan's people will not be sent to Shangjin. They will adopt an authorized operation method, and the original distribution system, corporate culture, and various management modes will remain unchanged.	no

“基金E账户”来了：证监会授权开发 投资者名下所有基金实现归集和查询 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	"Fund E-account" is here: CSRC authorizes development, all funds under investor's name can be consolidated and queried - Economic Observer Network - Professional Financial News Website	yes
经济观察网 记者 陈姗 基金购买渠道繁杂导致账户信息归集不易？	Economic Observer Network reporter Chen Shan: Is it difficult to consolidate account information due to the complex channels of fund purchase?	yes
总是遗忘“小金库”？	Always forgetting your "small treasury"?	yes
基民的这些问题即将得到解决。	These problems of fund investors are about to be solved.	yes
2月10日，证监会公告称，“基金E账户”APP在各手机应用商店上架并开展公开试运行。	On February 10, the CSRC announced that the "Fund E-account" APP has been launched in various mobile app stores and is undergoing public beta testing.	yes
据介绍，“基金E账户”为个人投资者提供公募基金账户及份额信息的“一站式”查询服务，旨在解决广大中小投资者遗忘账户、查询繁琐等行业服务痛点。	According to the introduction, the "Fund E-account" provides individual investors with a "one-stop" query service for public fund accounts and share information, aiming to solve the industry service pain points such as forgetting accounts and cumbersome queries for the majority of small and medium investors.	yes
据Wind数据显示，截至2022年底，国内共有公募基金管理人156家，管理基金规模约26万亿元；公募基金份额登记机构167家，公募基金销售机构411家。	According to Wind data, as of the end of 2022, there were 156 public fund managers in China, managing about 26 trillion yuan in funds; there were 167 public fund share registration institutions and 411 public fund sales institutions.	yes
各份额登记机构账户体系相互独立，缺乏行业统一的查询渠道。	The account systems of each share registration institution are independent of each other, lacking a unified industry query channel.	yes
有行业人士表示，2021年末我国基金投资者超过7.2亿人，也就是说，全国有一半人都投资了基金产品。	Some industry insiders said that by the end of 2021, there were more than 720 million fund investors in China, which means that half of the people in the country have invested in fund products.	yes
此前，投资者需要通过不同销售机构查询购买情况，而通过“基金E账户”可以查询所有销售渠道购买的情况，持有基金情况一目了然。	Previously, investors needed to query purchase conditions through different sales institutions, but through the "Fund E-account", they can query the purchase conditions of all sales channels, and the situation of holding funds is clear at a glance.	yes
“基金E账户”APP是什么？	What is the "Fund E-account" APP?	no
据相关文件介绍，“基金E账户”APP 是中国结算经中国证监会批准开发建设的公募基金行业门户手机应用，可为投资者提供全市场公募基金产品场外份额持有情况的一站式查询。	According to related documents, the "Fund E-account" APP is a public fund industry portal mobile application developed and built by China Settlement with the approval of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, which can provide investors with a one-stop query of the off-market shareholding situation of all market public fund products.	no
投资者可以通过“基金E账户”方便、快捷地掌握自己通过全市场各销售渠道购买的各基金管理人旗下公募基金产品场外份额的持有情况，全面提升查询效率。	Investors can conveniently and quickly grasp their own off-market shareholding situation of public fund products purchased through all market sales channels through the "Fund E-account", greatly improving the efficiency of queries.	no
具体来说，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”查询到的信息包括：在全市场各公募基金管理人处开立的基金账户信息、在公募基金销售机构处开立的交易账户信息以及持有的包括公开募集证券投资基金以及证券公司设立管理的投资者人数不受200人限制的集合资产管理计划等产品的场外份额持有情况。	Specifically, the information that investors can query through the "Fund E-account" includes: the fund account information opened at all public fund managers in the market, the trading account information opened at public fund sales institutions, and the off-market shareholding situation of products including publicly raised securities investment funds and collective asset management plans managed by securities companies with no limit on the number of investors.	no
上海证券基金评价研究中心业务负责人刘亦千向经济观察网记者表示，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”App一站式获知其所有的场外公募基金持有情况，帮助其找回“被遗忘的资产”，更重要的是为客户实现了综合基金投资情况的全账户信息归集，帮助客户更及时、准确、完整的掌握自身投资情况，从而更好地优化自身的基金组合配置，更好地规划自身的财务安排。	Liu Yiqian, the business head of the Shanghai Securities Fund Evaluation Research Center, told the Economic Observer Network reporter that investors can know all their off-market public fund holdings through the "Fund E-account" App, help them find "forgotten assets", and more importantly, it has realized the collection of all account information of comprehensive fund investment for customers, helping customers to grasp their own investment situation more timely, accurately and completely, so as to better optimize their own fund portfolio allocation and better plan their own financial arrangements.	no
如何注册使用？	How to register and use?	no
记者注意到，目前，“基金E账户”APP已在华为、苹果、小米、OPPO、vivo等手机应用商店上架，但APP尚处于公开试运行阶段，注册需要填写邀请码，投资者可以联系所持有基金的基金管理人获取。	The reporter noticed that at present, the "Fund E-account" APP has been launched in Huawei, Apple, Xiaomi, OPPO, vivo and other mobile app stores, but the APP is still in the public beta testing stage, registration requires an invitation code, investors can contact the fund manager of the fund they hold to obtain.	no
上海一家中大型公募基金客服人员向经济观察网记者提供了一个6位数的邀请码，并告诉记者，“APP试运行阶段，中国结算提供给每个基金管理人一定数量的邀请码，投资者电话过来获取，我们都会提供。	A customer service staff member of a medium and large public fund in Shanghai provided the Economic Observer Network reporter with a six-digit invitation code, and told the reporter, "During the APP beta testing stage, China Settlement provides each fund manager with a certain number of invitation codes. When investors call to get them, we will provide them.	no
等试运行结束后，开放用户注册时就不用邀请码了。	After the beta testing is over, when user registration is opened, no invitation code is needed.	no
”	"	no
记者根据证监会官网公示的“基金E账户”下载及使用说明相关文件进行了账户注册并完成查询，整个过程耗时仅几分钟，主要分为四步：用户注册、实名认证、基金账户绑定、公募基金查询。	The reporter registered an account and completed the query according to the "Fund E-account" download and use instructions related documents displayed on the CSRC official website. The whole process took only a few minutes, mainly divided into four steps: user registration, real-name authentication, fund account binding, and public fund query.	no
通过实名认证这一步之后，点击“资产”基金绑定按钮，记者通过各个基金销售平台购买的所有基金产品都呈现在绑定选项列表中（可绑定账户），完成绑定后就可以直观看到所投基金总资产并可以开始使用查询功能了。	After the real-name authentication step, click the "Asset" fund binding button, all the fund products purchased by the reporter through various fund sales platforms are presented in the binding option list (accounts that can be bound), after the binding is completed, you can directly see the total assets of the invested funds and can start using the query function.	no
值得注意的是，“基金E账户”仅为投资者提供查询服务，并不能进行申赎买卖。	It is worth noting that the "Fund E-account" only provides query services for investors and cannot carry out redemption transactions.	no
“基金 E 账户”所显示的数据日期一般为用户进行查询的日期（T日)往前推三个交易日。	The data date displayed by the "Fund E-account" is generally three trading days before the date the user queries (T day).	no
比如，在2 月10日打开“基金E账户”，资产页所显示的总资产、基金份额、基金净值对应日期为该日期往前推三个交易日，即2月7日。	For example, when you open the "Fund E-account" on February 10, the total assets, fund shares, and fund net value corresponding dates displayed on the asset page are three trading days before this date, that is, February 7.	no

中国云南省人类精子库9日发出宣传，征求大专以上学历者或在校生捐精，成功捐赠8至12次可获人民币4500元补贴。	On the 9th, the Human Sperm Bank of Yunnan Province, China, issued a call for donations from those with a college degree or above, or students, stating that successful donations 8 to 12 times could receive a subsidy of 4500 RMB.	yes
据台媒今天报道称，该讯息当日冲上微博热搜，并引发浙江、陕西、湖北、山东与北京等许多省市跟进倡议。	According to Taiwanese media reports today, the message quickly became a hot topic on Weibo, and sparked similar initiatives in many provinces and cities such as Zhejiang, Shaanxi, Hubei, Shandong, and Beijing.	yes

东德最后一位共产党总理今去世	The last Communist Prime Minister of East Germany passed away today.	yes
东德共产党的继任者在该党在一份声明中报告，“昨晚，汉斯·莫德罗 (Hans Modrow) 离开了我们，享年 95 岁。	The successors of the East German Communist Party reported in a statement, "Last night, Hans Modrow left us at the age of 95.	yes
因此，我们的党失去了一位重要领导人。	Thus, our party has lost an important leader.	yes
”	"	yes
1989 年 11 月 13 日，在将东柏林和西柏林分开 28 年的柏林墙打开四天后，莫德罗曾表示他将帮助把东德变成一个民主国家。	On November 13, 1989, four days after the Berlin Wall, which had separated East and West Berlin for 28 years, was opened, Modrow stated that he would help transform East Germany into a democratic country.	yes
当时，由于东德各地的抗议者要求民主和自由，共产党领导人被迫下台。	At that time, due to protesters across East Germany demanding democracy and freedom, the Communist Party leaders were forced to step down.	yes
戈尔巴乔夫 (Mikhail Gorbachev) 在苏联上台后曾要求在苏联主导的东欧也进行变革。	After Mikhail Gorbachev came to power in the Soviet Union, he called for reforms in Eastern Europe under Soviet leadership.	yes
1990 年 3 月，莫德罗宣布德意志民主共和国 (GDR) 的第一次也是唯一一次自由选举。	In March 1990, Modrow announced the first and only free election of the German Democratic Republic (GDR).	yes
选举结果导致他不再担任总理。	The election results led to him no longer serving as Prime Minister.	yes
尽管莫德罗进行了改革，但反对者指责他试图推迟 1990 年 10 月发生的政治变革和统一。	Although Modrow carried out reforms, opponents accused him of trying to delay the political changes and unification that occurred in October 1990.	yes
他还因试图重塑而不是废除秘密警察而受到批评。	He was also criticized for trying to reshape rather than abolish the secret police.	no
1993 年，莫德罗在 1989 年 5 月的市政选举中被判选举舞弊罪名成立，但并未入狱。	In 1993, Modrow was found guilty of election fraud in the municipal elections of May 1989, but was not imprisoned.	no
有称这些指控是出于政治动机。	Some say these charges were politically motivated.	no
1990 年至 1994 年，莫德罗继续在德国议会任职，并于 1999 年至 2004 年担任欧洲议会议员。	From 1990 to 1994, Modrow continued to serve in the German Parliament and was a member of the European Parliament from 1999 to 2004.	no

1999 年，他告诉路透社，他不希望旧东德回归，但表示应该承认东德的成就。	In 1999, he told Reuters that he did not want the old East Germany to return, but said that East Germany's achievements should be recognized.	no

第二次世界大战期间，他担任青年消防队排长，并在冲突快结束时成为纳粹民兵组织 Volkssturm 的一员，该组织征召 16 至 60 岁的男子参加最后的战争挣扎。	During World War II, he served as a youth fire brigade leader and became a member of the Nazi militia organization Volkssturm, which drafted men aged 16 to 60 for the final struggle of the war, as the conflict was nearing its end.	no

1949 年，即东德成立的那一年，他回国后找到了一份机械师的工作，并继续学习社会科学和经济学，并获得了博士学位。	In 1949, the year East Germany was established, he returned home to find a job as a mechanic, continued to study social sciences and economics, and earned a doctorate.	no

阿拉斯加上空被击落的 “物体”究竟是什么？	What exactly is the "object" shot down over Alaska?	yes
扑朔迷离，猜测纷纷	It's confusing, with many speculations.	yes
美国军方周五（2月10日）下午再次动用美国最先进的隐身喷气战机F-22击落了一个在美国阿拉斯加上空飞行的尚未确定身份的物体。	On Friday afternoon (February 10), the U.S. military once again used the most advanced stealth jet fighter F-22 to shoot down an unidentified object flying over Alaska.	yes
击落的地点距离阿拉斯加海岸十英里。	The location of the shootdown was ten miles off the coast of Alaska.	yes
这是美军在不到一周的时间里第二次击落空中飞行物体。	This is the second time in less than a week that the U.S. military has shot down an airborne object.	yes
上周六，来自中国的一个间谍气球在美国领空上漂移数日后在美国南卡罗莱纳州沿岸附近上空被击毁。	Last Saturday, a spy balloon from China was destroyed in the air near the coast of South Carolina after drifting over U.S. airspace for several days.	yes
五角大楼说，第二个被击落的物体于周四晚上首次进入美国领空，在阿拉斯加东北部上空移动时被美国军方跟踪，飞行高度为1.2万米（4万英尺），其大小与一辆小型汽车差不多，与先前被击落的那个中国间谍气球相比要小很多。	The Pentagon said that the second object shot down first entered U.S. airspace on Thursday night, was tracked by the U.S. military while moving over northeastern Alaska, flying at an altitude of 12,000 meters (40,000 feet), its size is about the same as a small car, much smaller than the previous Chinese spy balloon that was shot down.	yes
五角大楼还认为，目前没有迹象显示，这个物体是可操纵的。	The Pentagon also believes that there is currently no evidence to suggest that this object is controllable.	yes
白宫国家安全委员会战略沟通协调员约翰·科比周五表示，虽然这个在高空飞行的物体的具体样子尚不清楚，但它“对民航飞机的安全构成了合理的威胁”。	John Kirby, the White House National Security Council's strategic communications coordinator, said on Friday that although the exact appearance of this high-flying object is not clear, it "poses a reasonable threat to the safety of civil aircraft."	yes
科比表示，这个物体与美国境内发现的那个间谍气球不同，它上面没有悬挂“有效载荷”。	Kirby said that this object is different from the spy balloon found in the U.S., it does not have a "payload" hanging on it.	yes
科比说，“我们把它称为一个‘物体’是我们目前能够作出的最好的描述”。	Kirby said, "We call it an 'object' is the best description we can make at the moment."	no
拜登总统在下令击落这个物体之前听取了五角大楼的建议，他作出这个决定的时候“非常谨慎”，科比补充说。	President Biden ordered the shootdown of this object after listening to the advice of the Pentagon, he was "very cautious" when he made this decision, Kirby added.	no
美国官方对这个物体的描述大致可以归纳为：大小相当于一辆小汽车，没有操纵杆，没有悬挂装置，飞行高度为一万米左右。	The U.S. official description of this object can be summarized as: about the size of a small car, no joystick, no hanging device, flying at an altitude of about 10,000 meters.	no
但这些信息还无法回答基本问题，比如这个物体究竟是什么东西，它属于哪个国家，它在执行什么任务。	But this information still can't answer basic questions, such as what exactly is this object, which country does it belong to, and what mission is it carrying out.	no
目前网上许多的分析和猜测认为，这可能又是一只中国气球。	Many online analyses and speculations currently believe that this might be another Chinese balloon.	no
它可能与入侵美国领空的那只间谍气球和在拉美上空飘动的那只中国气球一样都来自中国，它们在不同地点执行某种任务。	It may come from China like the spy balloon that invaded U.S. airspace and the Chinese balloon floating over Latin America, they are carrying out some kind of mission at different locations.	no
也有人把阿拉斯加的这个“物体”与“不明飞行物”（UFO）联系在一起。	Some people have linked this "object" in Alaska with "Unidentified Flying Objects" (UFOs).	no
美国新闻周刊的报道引用美国前众议员彼得·梅杰（Peter Meijer）周五在推特上发出的推文说，“真希望这个‘不明飞行物’也是一个间谍气球，而不是一个合法的UFO”。	A report in Newsweek quoted a tweet from former U.S. Representative Peter Meijer on Friday saying, "I really hope this 'unidentified flying object' is also a spy balloon, not a legitimate UFO."	no
“将外星飞船与气象气球混为一谈的讽刺意味很令人惊讶，但这不值得引发一场星际冲突，”梅杰说。	"The irony of conflating alien spacecraft with weather balloons is surprising, but it's not worth triggering an interstellar conflict," Meijer said.	no
梅杰是在科比证实阿拉斯加的这个物体被击落之后不久发出这个推文的。	Meijer tweeted this shortly after Kirby confirmed that the object in Alaska had been shot down.	no
新闻周刊说，怀疑这个物体是UFO的不止是梅杰一人。	Newsweek said that Meijer is not the only one who suspects that this object is a UFO.	no

我想，这个小说集，以及它的标题，像是一种行为艺术，作者想表达的是，爱情不止是舞台上的悲欢离合，都市传说中的海枯石烂，也不只是你侬我侬的如胶似漆，爱情不止是以上也不应该被以上代表，爱情也是平淡如水的生活，枯燥无味的日复一日，也有对生活的无措，现实的逃避，未来的茫然。	I think, this collection of short stories, and its title, is like a kind of performance art. What the author wants to express is that love is not only the joys and sorrows on the stage, the eternal love in urban legends, nor just the inseparable intimacy between you and me. Love is not only the above but should not be represented by the above. Love is also a plain life like water, a boring day after day, and there is also a sense of helplessness in life, the escape from reality, and the confusion about the future.	yes
